            url: "https://cdn.cookielaw.org/scripttemplates/202404.1.0/otBannerSdk.js",
            options: {},
        }

        const countriesWithOneTrustEnabled = {"countries":["ES","MX","PH","TH","TR"]};

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadOneTrustScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();

            if (!shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            preloadBannerSdk();

            ONE_TRUST_LIBRARIES.forEach((library) => {
                loadScript(library.url, "text/javascript", library.options);
            });

            if (country === "US") {
                loadCCPAAddon();
            }
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithOneTrustEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithOneTrustEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithOneTrustEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            script.setAttribute("data-domain-script", DATA_DOMAIN_SCRIPT);

            return script;
        }

        function loadCCPAAddon() {
            loadScript(CCPA_ADDON.url, "text/javascript", CCPA_ADDON.options);
        }

        function preloadBannerSdk() {
            const link = document.createElement("link");
            link.href = BANNER_SDK.url;
            link.rel = "preload";
            link.as = "script";

            document.head.appendChild(link);
        }

        function oneTrustLoaded() {
            return !!(window.OneTrust || window.OneTrustStub);
        }

        console.debug('OneTrust setup', countriesWithOneTrustEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !oneTrustLoaded()) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!oneTrustLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (function () {
        function shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            const countriesWithKetchEnabled = {"countries":["IN","HU","SG"]};
            if (!countriesWithKetchEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithKetchEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }
            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithKetchEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }


        function loadKetchScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            if (!shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            window.semaphore = window.semaphore || [];

            window.ketch = function () {
                window.semaphore.push(arguments);
            };

            var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(document.location.search);
            var property = urlParams.has("property") ? urlParams.get("property") : "website_smart_tag";

            var scriptElement = document.createElement("script");
            scriptElement.type = "text/javascript";
            scriptElement.src = "https://global.ketchcdn.com/web/v2/config/fandom/" + property + "/boot.js";
            scriptElement.defer = scriptElement.async = true;

            document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(scriptElement);
        }

        function ketchLoaded() {
            return !!window.ketch;
        }

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !ketchLoaded()) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!ketchLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (async function () {
        // const AIRGAP_URL = '<script
        // data-cfasync="false"
        // src=""
        const AIRGAP_URL = 'https://transcend-cdn.com/cm/54b0c313-5d22-47e5-92fd-f979a37d1ad0/airgap.js';
        const countriesWithAirgapEnabled = [];

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {

            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadAirgapScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            const enabled = shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) || airgapScriptForced();

            if (!enabled) {
                return;
            }

            loadScript(AIRGAP_URL, "text/javascript", {
                'data-cfasync': false
            });
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithAirgapEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function airgapScriptForced() {
            return window.location.search.includes('icPreferredCMP=airgap');
        }

        function shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithAirgapEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithAirgapEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            return script;
        }

        console.debug('Airgap setup', countriesWithAirgapEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        let geo = getGeo();

        if (geo === null) {
            geo = await waitForGeo();
        }

        if (geo) {
            loadAirgapScripts(geo);
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
	const useMaxDefaultContentWidth = Boolean(false);

	const defaultContentWidth = useMaxDefaultContentWidth ? 'expanded' : 'collapsed';

	let contentWidthPreference;

	try {
		contentWidthPreference = localStorage.getItem('contentwidth') || defaultContentWidth;
	} catch (e) {
		contentWidthPreference = defaultContentWidth;
	}

	if ( contentWidthPreference === 'expanded' ) {
		document.documentElement.classList.add('is-content-expanded');
	}
</script>

													<script data-name="featured-video-mapped-to-wiki">
	(function () {
		// we can't use mw.config here because it's too early so we need to pass this data in different way
		const videoDetails = {
			mapping: {"mediaId":"sXWp3rZ0","connatixPlaylistId":"36081eca-e784-4e30-87c3-133cf673e447","impressionsPerSession":4},
			impressionsPerSession: 4,
		};
		const videoBridgeCountries = ["AE","AG","AL","AM","AR","AT","AU","AZ","BA","BB","BD","BG","BH","BN","BO","BR","BS","BY","CA","CH","CL","CN","CO","CR","CU","CY","CZ","DE","DK","DO","DZ","EC","EE","EG","ES","FI","FR","GB","GE","GF","GG","GH","GP","GR","GT","GU","GY","HK","HN","HR","HU","ID","IE","IL","IM","IN","IQ","IR","IS","IT","JE","JM","JO","JP","KE","KG","KH","KR","KW","KY","KZ","LA","LB","LK","LT","LU","LV","LY","MA","MD","ME","MK","MM","MN","MO","MQ","MT","MU","MV","MX","MY","NG","NI","NO","NP","NZ","OM","PA","PE","PH","PK","PL","PR","PS","PT","PY","QA","RE","RO","RS","RU","SA","SC","SE","SG","SI","SK","SV","TD","TH","TN","TR","TT","TW","UA","US","UY","UZ","VE","VI","VN","ZA","ZW"];
		const tier3VideoBridgeCountries = ["GB","BE","NL","DE","AU","MX","AR","FR","MD","CA","ES","IT","PE","CO","CL","NZ"];
		let hasVideoOnPage = null;

		function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
			const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
			return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
		}

		function hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki() {
			const impressionsSoFar = Number(getCookieValue('playerImpressionsInWiki')) || 0;
			const allowedImpressions = Number(videoDetails.impressionsPerSession);

			return impressionsSoFar >= allowedImpressions;
		}

		function getCountryCode() {
			try {
				return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo'))).country.toLowerCase();
			} catch {
				return null;
			}
		}

		function isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() {
			const countryCode = getCountryCode();

			if (!countryCode) {
				return false;
			}

			// If it's a default mapping, then check the country whitelist from the default mapping.
			if (videoDetails?.mapping?.isDefaultMapping) {
				// If the wiki is classified as a tier3 wiki, then check the country whitelist from the tier3VideoBridge whitelist.
				const allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis = tier3VideoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedTier3CountryCode) {
					return allowedTier3CountryCode.toLowerCase();
				})

				return allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			} else {
				// If not a default mapping wiki (so it's a wiki mapping), then check the country whitelist from the videoBridge whitelist
				const allowedCountries = videoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedCountryCode) {
					return allowedCountryCode.toLowerCase();
				});

				return allowedCountries.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			}
		}

		window.fandomIsVideoPossible = function () {
			if (hasVideoOnPage === null) {
				hasVideoOnPage =
					videoDetails.mapping &&
					isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() &&
					!hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki();
			}

			return hasVideoOnPage;
		};

		window.canPlayVideo = function () {
			return window.fandomIsVideoPossible()
		};

		if (!window.canPlayVideo()) {
			document.body.classList.add('no-featured-video');
		} else {
			document.body.classList.add('has-featured-video');
		}
	})();
</script>

</section>
</aside>

</p><p><b>Monkey D. Garp</b>,<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">[12]</a></sup> also known as <b>"Garp the Fist"</b>,<sup id="cite_ref-intro_7-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-intro-7">[7]</a></sup> is an extremely famous and powerful <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marine</a> <a href="/wiki/Vice_Admiral" title="Vice Admiral">Vice Admiral</a>. He is the father of <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Dragon" title="Monkey D. Dragon">Monkey D. Dragon</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-GarpandDragon_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GarpandDragon-13">[13]</a></sup> the paternal grandfather of <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-Grandfather_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Grandfather-14">[14]</a></sup> and the adoptive grandfather of <a href="/wiki/Portgas_D._Ace" title="Portgas D. Ace">Portgas D. Ace</a>. He was responsible for overseeing Ace's birth and raising a young Luffy, before entrusting them both to the <a href="/wiki/Dadan_Family" title="Dadan Family">Dadan Family</a>.
</p><p>Garp is a major figure, along with <a href="/wiki/Kong" title="Kong">Kong</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sengoku" title="Sengoku">Sengoku</a>, <a href="/wiki/Shiki" title="Shiki">Shiki</a>, <a href="/wiki/Silvers_Rayleigh" title="Silvers Rayleigh">Silvers Rayleigh</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tsuru" title="Tsuru">Tsuru</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a>, from the times when <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a>, the "Pirate King", was still alive. His feats as a Marine soldier gained him immense notoriety and prestige, with his actions during the <a href="/wiki/God_Valley_Incident" title="God Valley Incident">God Valley Incident</a> in particular bestowing him the title of <b>"Hero of the Marines"</b>. Notably, Garp was offered the rank of <a href="/wiki/Admiral" title="Admiral">Admiral</a> several times throughout his career, but he refused the offer of promotion every time due to his deep hatred and contempt for <a href="/wiki/World_Noble" title="World Noble">World Nobles</a>. He is also the former mentor of <a href="/wiki/Kuzan" title="Kuzan">Kuzan</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">[15]</a></sup>
</p><p>After Ace's death at the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">Summit War of Marineford</a>, Garp became a Marine Instructor to train new recruits.<sup id="cite_ref-instructor_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-instructor-5">[5]</a></sup> While the public believes him to be retired, he still retains the rank of Vice Admiral.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">[16]</a></sup> During his mission to rescue Koby from the <a href="/wiki/Blackbeard_Pirates" title="Blackbeard Pirates">Blackbeard Pirates</a>, Garp was badly injured and imprisoned on <a href="/wiki/Hachinosu" title="Hachinosu">Hachinosu</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-c1126_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1126-17">[17]</a></sup> being officially declared "missing in action" by the Marines.<sup id="cite_ref-c1088_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1088-18">[18]</a></sup>
</p><p>Garp was first introduced during the <a href="/wiki/Diary_of_Koby-Meppo" title="Diary of Koby-Meppo">Diary of Koby-Meppo</a> Cover Page Serial, where he took charge of both <a href="/wiki/Koby" title="Koby">Koby</a> and <a href="/wiki/Helmeppo" title="Helmeppo">Helmeppo</a>'s training after its events. Due to his actions, he could be considered the main antagonist of the <a href="/wiki/Post-Enies_Lobby_Arc" title="Post-Enies Lobby Arc">Post-Enies Lobby Arc</a> and a supporting antagonist in the <a href="/wiki/Marineford_Arc" title="Marineford Arc">Marineford Arc</a>.
</p>

			<h3 class="trfc161__header-text">Quick Answers</h3>
		</div>
		<img class="trfc161-logo" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/8941553e-df6a-4310-a080-b9da56fdcbdd" alt="fandom logo">
	</div>
	<div class="trfc161__groups">
			<details class="trfc161__group " data-question-id="8184" data-revision-id="2">
				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">What is the significance of Garp's nickname 'Garp the Fist'?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						Garp's nickname 'Garp the Fist' is a testament to his immense physical strength and fighting prowess. He is known for his devastating punch attacks, one of which is the 'Galaxy Impact' that can create massive explosions and even destroy an entire island. Garp earned this epithet after defeating formidable opponents like Don Chinjao, who was known to split a continent with a headbutt, with just a single punch. Even at an advanced age, Garp's power remains undiminished, striking fear into the hearts of pirates and earning him the respect of his peers in the One Piece universe.
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Fandom
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>
				</div>
			</details>
			<details class="trfc161__group " data-question-id="8185" data-revision-id="3">
				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">How did Monkey D. Garp become a Vice Admiral in One Piece?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						Monkey D. Garp, also known as 'Garp the Fist', joined the Marines at the age of 22 and over the years, he rose up through the ranks due to his exceptional strength and heroism. His journey to becoming a Vice Admiral is marked by numerous battles and victories. Despite his descendants Dragon and Luffy being among the world's most infamous figures, Garp's dedication to justice and his 'galaxy impact' in the Marine forces earned him the respect and rank of Vice Admiral.
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Community
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>
				</div>
			</details>
			<details class="trfc161__group " data-question-id="8186" data-revision-id="2">
				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">What is the relationship between Garp and Monkey D. Luffy?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						Monkey D. Garp is the grandfather of Monkey D. Luffy. As a vice admiral and a hero of the Marines, Garp had high hopes for his grandson and wanted him to follow in his footsteps. However, Luffy chose the path of piracy, much to Garp's disappointment. Despite this, Garp cares deeply for Luffy and often finds himself torn between his duty as a Marine and his love for his grandson.
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Fandom
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>
				</div>
			</details>
			<details class="trfc161__group " data-question-id="8188" data-revision-id="3">
				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">Who did Garp entrust the upbringing of Ace and Luffy to?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						Monkey D. Garp, the renowned Vice Admiral, entrusted the upbringing of Ace and Luffy to a close friend of his, the mountain bandit Curly Dadan. Despite his tough love and high expectations for them to become strong Marines, both boys had their hearts set on the pirate life. Garp's unique training methods, which included leaving Luffy in a jungle in the middle of the night, were all part of his plan to make them strong and resilient. However, their paths diverged from Garp's vision, much to his chagrin.
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Community
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>
				</div>
			</details>
	</div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Appearance">Appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D1&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Garp is a tall, tanned, broad-chested, muscular old man. He has a beard and a scar over his left eye. In the anime, his eye color is blue, and his hair is gray, whereas in the manga, it is white. Garp and <a href="/wiki/Tsuru" title="Tsuru">Tsuru</a> are the only two Vice Admirals to have special shoulder-pads; Garp is golden and blue (black and red in the anime) while Tsuru is purple with white dot whereas the standard color is blue and red. During the Battle of Edd War, Garp's had two black stripes on his epaulettes, and during his appearance at Water 7, it increased to three stripes and by the time of the Marineford War, it increased again to four stripes.
</p><p>The dog mask that Garp initially wore when introduced served to hide his identity as Luffy's grandfather, whose design had appeared in <i><a href="/wiki/Romance_Dawn,_Version_2" title="Romance Dawn, Version 2">Romance Dawn, Version 2</a></i>. After their relationship was revealed in the <a href="/wiki/Post-Enies_Lobby_Arc" title="Post-Enies Lobby Arc">Post-Enies Lobby Arc</a>, Garp is no longer seen wearing the mask.
</p><p>In his free time or vacation, Garp often wears sandals, a red tropical shirt and light-colored shorts. He sometimes pairs this shirt with black trousers and boots.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">[19]</a></sup> When visiting Dadan during Luffy's childhood, he sometimes wears his official black suit without wearing his Marine cape.
</p><p>Thirty-eight years ago, Garp's hair was all black and lacked a goatee. He wore a white dress shirt and a red tie.
</p><p>Thirty years ago, Garp's hair and goatee were all black. He wore a dark suit with an orange striped undershirt and a black tie.
</p><p>Twenty-four years ago, Garp's hair and goatee were still black, with sideburns beginning to whiten. He wore a dark double-breasted suit with a white shirt and a red necktie.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">[20]</a></sup>
</p><p>When he was a child and a young man, Garp resembled Luffy, though more muscular than his grandson. As a child, he had light brown hair, wore a tropical button shirt with shorts, and wielded a pipe staff. Garp already had the scar on his left eye in his childhood days.
</p><p>After the timeskip, his appearance has somewhat remained the same though he now wears a dark-colored suit (still white in the anime).
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality">Personality</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D7&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">Don't be tied down by this nonsense!! I taught you to live in the moment!!!! Listen up, Kuzan!! Wavering is a sign of weakness!!!!</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;">— Garp to Kuzan.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">[21]</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p>Garp is an eccentric but righteous and caring man, who is loyal to both his criminal family and the Marine Headquarters, who he has served for decades. He is loud, boisterous, exuberant, and overall acts in a similar manner to his grandson, however he can be very serious if the situation requires it, for example in combat against an enemy (this can be seen when he faced the pirate Shiki alongside Sengoku, and also more recently when he had to fight against Aokiji, his former pupil). He has a habit of falling asleep during conversations and can be absent-minded. Luffy's crew noted his apparently hereditary selfishness during Garp's interaction with Luffy in Water 7.
</p><p>Despite being a righteous man, Garp takes great pride in being a Marine despite knowing how corrupt the Marines are under the World Government, and wanted his family to follow his footsteps, as his son Dragon previously joined the Marines but left due to being disgusted by their corruption and hypocrisy, he also harshly trained his grandsons in order to make them splendid Marines and would beat them up whenever they defied his wishes by wanting to be pirates.
</p><p>Garp is aware of the World Government's immense corruption and tyrannical influence over the world and society, particularly of the Celestial Dragons' cruelty and oppression of civilians but held a lenient and laid-back stance on it, believing as long as there is no open bloodshed, even if there are social discrimination and political corruption, he can call it peace, contrary to his son's rebellious stance against political corruption.
</p><p>Unlike many Marines, Garp does not believe that a person's lineage determines their path. On a similar note, he does not believe that being labeled a criminal necessarily makes someone a bad person. Although Garp wanted his grandsons to become Marines, he entrusted their care to a <a href="/wiki/Curly_Dadan" title="Curly Dadan">mountain bandit</a> whom he had refused to turn over for prosecution.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/8f/Fist_of_Love.png/revision/latest?cb=20220928135503" class="image"><img alt="Fist of Love" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Fist of Love.png" data-image-key="Fist_of_Love.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/8f/Fist_of_Love.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220928135503"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/8f/Fist_of_Love.png/revision/latest?cb=20220928135503" class="image"><img alt="Fist of Love" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/8f/Fist_of_Love.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220928135503" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Fist of Love.png" data-image-key="Fist_of_Love.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/8f/Fist_of_Love.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220928135503"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Fist_of_Love.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Garp's "Fist of Love"</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Garp believes that throwing children into harsh conditions will ultimately make them strong and has no problem striking children to drive home a point. His grandson, Luffy, for example, stated that Garp almost killed him several times when he was a child under the guise of making him strong. Despite this, Garp is a supportive person. When Ace asked Garp whether he should have been born, Garp replies that Ace will find the answer if he continues living. When Momousagi mentioned Luffy being targeted by two Emperors, Garp did not express much concern about it.
</p><p>His harsh discipline extends to himself as he forced himself through an extremely harsh and unorthodox training method of punching battleships since his youth.
</p><p>Although Garp will ultimately comply with Marine HQ's most serious orders, he highly values his freedom and family. Often to a point where he bends the rules to accommodate these values. He initially refused to capture Luffy in Water 7 until explicitly ordered to do so. Despite fulfilling his duties, Garp has a strong Moral Code to follow, which according to Sengoku is the main reason why Garp refused the promotion as an Admiral multiple times, as his code dictates that it is not his duty to protect Celestial Dragons. Additionally, Garp is generally amused by Luffy's exploits as a pirate, and only seriously laments both of his grandsons' choices to become pirates after Ace is captured. He ultimately allowed Luffy to hit him due to valuing his family more than his duty as a Marine during the war at Marineford. He even seemed ready to defend them when Akainu executed Ace and was on the verge of killing Luffy.
</p><p>Like Luffy, Garp is extremely blunt and honest when talking to people as seen when he openly badmouthed <a href="/wiki/Sterry" title="Sterry">Sterry</a>, the current king of the Goa Kingdom, unafraid of the consequences. He considers the Celestial Dragons scumbags and is not afraid of expressing this vocally. The main reason he refused to become an admiral is because he does not want to be their direct subordinate. On one occasion, he also blurted out Monkey D. Dragon's name in front of Luffy, his friends, and his subordinates without any consideration at Water 7. When he realized he should not have said that he just simply laughed it off, and shamelessly asked those who heard it to forget it.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">[22]</a></sup>
</p><p>Garp believes in the potential of youth and sees it as a Marine's duty to protect the future. This is the first lesson he teaches to Marine recruits, even telling them in a situation where they have to choose between saving an old man and a baby; they should leave the old man behind on the dangerous island and save the baby because the old man doesn't have much time left while the baby and them have a whole future ahead of them. While his fellow Marine instructor told him never to repeat this lesson, Garp stood by it. He would display his commitment to this by launching a rescue mission to save Koby after he was taken to Hachinosu by Blackbeard, declaring Koby the future of the Marines. At the end of the raid, he showed his faith in Koby, <a href="/wiki/Prince_Grus" title="Prince Grus">Prince Grus</a> and <a href="/wiki/Helmeppo" title="Helmeppo">Helmeppo</a> by entrusting them to save the Marine ship from <a href="/wiki/Avalo_Pizarro" title="Avalo Pizarro">Avalo Pizarro</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Shima_Shima_no_Mi" title="Shima Shima no Mi">attack</a> while he stayed behind to allow them to escape, calling all of them the "future of the Marines".<sup id="cite_ref-c1088_18-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1088-18">[18]</a></sup>
</p><p>When Garp prepares to fight seriously, he often removes his Marine coat<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">[23]</a></sup> or a suit jacket.<sup id="cite_ref-c438p11_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c438p11-24">[24]</a></sup> Like his grandson, Garp is extremely fond of food, especially donuts, rice crackers and meat.
</p><p>Garp has his own <a href="/wiki/Laughter_Style" title="Laughter Style">laughter style</a>: Bwahaha or Wahaha.
</p><p>Garp follows "My Justice"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">おれの正義</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Ore no Seigi</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-vc2_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vc2-25">[25]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Marines">Marines</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D9&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>As the "Hero of the Marines", Garp is overall very well-respected for cornering the <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Pirate King</a> multiple times. While Garp seems devoted to his duties, he has his own sense of justice and does not always obey orders which are given to him. Both Garp's immense popularity and achievements are noted by Sengoku to be the reason Garp was never disposed of for his rebellious attitude. He was requested to remain behind as an instructor due to his fame, which will be invaluable in recruiting, Garp has problems with respecting his superiors and such is the case with then-Fleet Admiral <a href="/wiki/Kong" title="Kong">Kong</a> 27 years ago, and former Fleet Admiral Sengoku. Even including the fact that Garp was about to try to kill Akainu for killing Ace, it seems that this has not affected Garp's standing in the Marines even after his relationship with both Dragon and Luffy was revealed to the world, as Kong insisted that Garp's title and records can be utilized to recruit new Marines.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Crew">Crew</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D10&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Garp's crew often reacts with shock or uncertainty to his behavior. At times he seems to be unaware of the true extent of what is going on around him. After ordering his crew to rebuild a wall that Garp himself had just destroyed, his crew refused to do so unless he helped as well. This insubordinate behavior was displayed amongst a Marine crew, but Garp complied with their demand. Despite Garp telling his crew about his relationship with Luffy and Dragon, most Marines were unaware of it until the war with Whitebeard, suggesting that his men kept it a secret.
</p><p>Garp's right hand man is a Marine of unknown rank, who is usually seen with him. In the anime, his name is <a href="/wiki/Bogard" title="Bogard">Bogard</a>, although his name has not been revealed in the manga as of yet. It seems that Garp and Bogard have been together for at least 38 years.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Koby_and_Helmeppo">Koby and Helmeppo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D11&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Additionally, Garp is the mentor of <a href="/wiki/Koby" title="Koby">Koby</a> and <a href="/wiki/Helmeppo" title="Helmeppo">Helmeppo</a>, who both came to admire him. He was shocked when Koby shouted out to stop the killing at Marineford during the war with Whitebeard.
</p><p>When Koby was captured by the Blackbeard Pirates after his failed attempt to arrest <a href="/wiki/Boa_Hancock" title="Boa Hancock">Boa Hancock</a>, he plans on going to rescue him, disregarding protocol. Garp acknowledged Koby to be his beloved pupil. Due to knowing Koby's relentless determination and effort during the early days of his training, Garp had high expectations for Koby calling him the future of the Marines. Upon seeing Koby awaken his potential by destroying Pizzaro's giant Island hand, Garp wholeheartedly laughed, content to witness his beloved pupil's growth.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Sengoku">Sengoku</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D12&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f9/Garp_and_Sengoku.png/revision/latest?cb=20230507213433" class="image"><img alt="Garp and Sengoku" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Garp and Sengoku.png" data-image-key="Garp_and_Sengoku.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f9/Garp_and_Sengoku.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230507213433"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f9/Garp_and_Sengoku.png/revision/latest?cb=20230507213433" class="image"><img alt="Garp and Sengoku" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f9/Garp_and_Sengoku.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230507213433" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Garp and Sengoku.png" data-image-key="Garp_and_Sengoku.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f9/Garp_and_Sengoku.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230507213433"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Garp_and_Sengoku.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">A typical moment between Garp and Sengoku.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As a hero of the Marines, Garp commands high respect among the Marines, even from then-<a href="/wiki/Marine_Ranks#Fleet_Admiral" title="Marine Ranks">Fleet Admiral</a> <a href="/wiki/Sengoku" title="Sengoku">Sengoku</a>. In the past, Garp and Sengoku seemed to be very good friends, albeit that Sengoku was a little annoyed with Garp's tendency to act of his own accord whenever Roger was involved. Currently, as with the revelation that both <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> and <a href="/wiki/Portgas_D._Ace" title="Portgas D. Ace">Portgas D. Ace</a> are Garp's grandsons (Ace being adopted), as well as Luffy's multiple actions in such a short time, Sengoku has begun losing patience with Garp. But the two Marines still share a close friendship even though Sengoku is often exasperated at Garp's antics, like his offering of tea to Sengoku and <a href="/wiki/Bartholomew_Kuma" title="Bartholomew Kuma">Kuma</a> while discussing Luffy's actions at <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark" title="Thriller Bark">Thriller Bark</a>.
</p><p>Garp, on the other hand, seems to merely laugh it off and enjoys getting on Sengoku's nerves. Notably, Sengoku's biggest annoyance was Garp's refusal to keep his family under control even when threatened with the consequences. Garp simply does not believe the life of an old man could ever atone for the actions of his family. When or how long Sengoku knew of Garp adopting Ace is unknown, but Sengoku found out that Ace is the son of <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a>. Also, how long Sengoku knew about Luffy and Dragon's familial relationship to Garp is unknown, but Sengoku had no problem revealing all of it worldwide.
</p><p>When Garp allowed Luffy to land a punch on him to save Ace, many of the surrounding Marines were shocked to see what they believe to be an impossibility: the legendary Garp was easily defeated by a rookie. Sengoku, however, was able to tell of Garp's hesitancy, and was displeased that he chose family over duty.
</p><p>After the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">Summit War of Marineford</a>, Garp and Sengoku retired but their records remained untouched.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Tsuru">Tsuru</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D13&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Garp is well acquainted with <a href="/wiki/Tsuru" title="Tsuru">Tsuru</a> having known her for a long time. Before the Summit War of Marineford occurred, she told him that he had done nothing wrong regarding Ace, which Garp replied to with laughter, saying that she was supposed to be sympathetic towards him during this situation.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Sakazuki">Sakazuki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D14&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Sakazuki did not show any respect to Garp despite the old <a href="/wiki/Vice_Admiral" title="Vice Admiral">Vice Admiral</a> being a "Hero of the Marines" who was eligible for the position of admiral due to him being from the previous generation, but mostly for sharing the same lineage with criminals like Dragon and Luffy.​​ Garp in turn also has no respect for Sakazuki even though he is now the fleet admiral, nor does he consider it. He claimed to Sengoku that he would have mercilessly killed Sakazuki for executing Ace if he was not restrained by the former.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="World_Government">World Government</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D15&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kong">Kong</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D16&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Garp and Kong are well acquainted with each other, due to the latter being the former Fleet Admiral years ago. Kong respects Garp's abilities, as he always insisted that Garp accept the promotion to Admiral, but Garp constantly declined. They remain acquainted even after Kong became the Commander-in-Chief for the World Government. After the Marineford War, Kong reassigned Garp to the rank of Marine Instructor after he succeeded in persuading Garp to stay in the Marines and train new recruits.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="World_Nobles">World Nobles</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D17&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Though he is a Marine and is loyal to the World Government, Garp is disgusted by the World Nobles and refused the promotion to admiral due to the fact it would make him their direct subordinate.<sup id="cite_ref-c957p9_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c957p9-26">[26]</a></sup> He has no hesitancy in degrading the Celestial Dragons in front of others of importance, such as <a href="/wiki/King_(Title)" title="King (Title)">King</a> <a href="/wiki/Sterry" title="Sterry">Sterry</a>, only halfheartedly taking back the insult and went as far as directly calling them scumbags for their cruel and heinous natures. The only reason why the World Nobles did not dispose of him for his rebellious personality was due to his popularity and merits.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Family">Family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D18&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Monkey_D._Dragon">Monkey D. Dragon</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D19&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Dragon" title="Monkey D. Dragon">Dragon</a> is Garp's son.<sup id="cite_ref-GarpandDragon_13-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GarpandDragon-13">[13]</a></sup> No direct interactions between the two have been shown. In the past, he expressed discontent about his own son leaving the Marines and becoming a <a href="/wiki/Revolutionary_Army" title="Revolutionary Army">Revolutionary</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">[27]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">[28]</a></sup> though over the years he seems much more casual about his son's path as a Revolutionary who is wanted by the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a>. There appears to be some sort of understanding between the two, as Garp was aware that the reason Dragon was in <a href="/wiki/Loguetown" title="Loguetown">Loguetown</a> was to see Luffy set off for the <a href="/wiki/Grand_Line" title="Grand Line">Grand Line</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">[29]</a></sup> After the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">Summit War of Marineford</a>, he was not fazed by the fact that his relationship with Dragon became public knowledge. It also seems his reputation as a hero hasn’t been tarnished by this revelation.
</p><p>Garp and Dragon have different assessments of the East Blue. While Garp perceives it as a rather peaceful place, Dragon expresses his disgust with Garp's view of "peace" as nothing more than a form of oppression authorized by the law in places, such as <a href="/wiki/Tequila_Wolf" title="Tequila Wolf">Tequila Wolf</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Goa_Kingdom" title="Goa Kingdom">Goa Kingdom</a>, where common people live in horrible conditions.
</p><p>Ultimately, Garp has an extremely different ideology from his son. While Garp takes pride and contentment in being a Marine serving the World Government, Dragon absolutely despises the World Government to the point of becoming a Revolutionary and seeking to overthrow them. However, they are unified in one belief – disdain toward the <a href="/wiki/World_Noble" title="World Noble">Celestial Dragons</a>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Monkey_D._Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D20&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/12/Ace%2C_Dragon%2C_Garp%2C_and_Luffy_on_Newspaper.png/revision/latest?cb=20220913094501" class="image"><img alt="Ace, Dragon, Garp, and Luffy on Newspaper" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="242" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ace, Dragon, Garp, and Luffy on Newspaper.png" data-image-key="Ace%2C_Dragon%2C_Garp%2C_and_Luffy_on_Newspaper.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/12/Ace%2C_Dragon%2C_Garp%2C_and_Luffy_on_Newspaper.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220913094501"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/12/Ace%2C_Dragon%2C_Garp%2C_and_Luffy_on_Newspaper.png/revision/latest?cb=20220913094501" class="image"><img alt="Ace, Dragon, Garp, and Luffy on Newspaper" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/12/Ace%2C_Dragon%2C_Garp%2C_and_Luffy_on_Newspaper.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220913094501" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="242" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ace, Dragon, Garp, and Luffy on Newspaper.png" data-image-key="Ace%2C_Dragon%2C_Garp%2C_and_Luffy_on_Newspaper.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/12/Ace%2C_Dragon%2C_Garp%2C_and_Luffy_on_Newspaper.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220913094501"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ace,_Dragon,_Garp,_and_Luffy_on_Newspaper.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Garp appears on the news about Luffy's return.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Garp raised his grandson <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a> and sets high standards for him,<sup id="cite_ref-Grandfather_14-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Grandfather-14">[14]</a></sup> and gets mad at the slightest mistake he makes, even when his own are sometimes no better (i.e., telling off Luffy for falling asleep only to fall asleep himself). This often leads Luffy to receiving the force of Garp's punches, and due to these experiences, he has become afraid of his grandfather. Garp also claims Luffy was poisoned by <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Shanks</a> with ideas of becoming a pirate, as Garp wanted Luffy to be a great Marine like him. Luffy, however, claims otherwise and told Garp that even as a child he wanted to be a <a href="/wiki/Pirate" title="Pirate">pirate</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">[30]</a></sup> Nevertheless, the two get along quite well. As <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a> stated at the time of Garp's departure, that there seems to be an amazing ego that runs in Garp's family. Garp left Luffy in Dadan's care as a child, which is how Luffy met Ace.
</p><p>Garp appears proud when Luffy commits outrageous acts and found it amusing when he learned that Luffy had infiltrated the great prison Impel Down in an attempt to rescue Ace. When he learned that Luffy had broken out of Impel Down (taking many infamous prisoners along with him) and headed straight to Marineford, where the marines were currently waging war against Whitebeard and his crew, Garp was shocked. He was even more shocked when Luffy, along with an entire battleship of prisoners, fell off a frozen tsunami and into the war front.
</p><p>This shows that he cares for his grandson's well-being. He later calmed himself as the battle went on and simply watched as Luffy fought the marines, throughout which he seemed distraught whenever Luffy was struck down by various powerful soldiers. When Sengoku made Luffy's relationship to Dragon public, Garp simply states that Luffy already has such widespread notoriety that his connection to Dragon is irrelevant. Garp expressed surprise at Luffy's ability to use <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Haoshokou Haki</a> before commenting that Luffy inherited it after all. When Luffy was on the verge of saving Ace, Garp blocked him and refused to move, citing his Marine duties. Despite this, Garp allowed Luffy to hit him without fighting back.
</p><p>After the timeskip, Garp does not seem to be troubled by his grandson's growing infamy. This was demonstrated when he was not the least bit concerned that two of the <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Four Emperors</a> are after him, even laughing at the idea of the emperors actually teaming up over something.<sup id="cite_ref-c907_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c907-31">[31]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Portgas_D._Ace">Portgas D. Ace</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D21&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 220px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b7/Ace_and_Garp_in_Impel_Down.png/revision/latest?cb=20230601050849" class="image"><img alt="Ace and Garp in Impel Down" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ace and Garp in Impel Down.png" data-image-key="Ace_and_Garp_in_Impel_Down.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b7/Ace_and_Garp_in_Impel_Down.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20230601050849"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b7/Ace_and_Garp_in_Impel_Down.png/revision/latest?cb=20230601050849" class="image"><img alt="Ace and Garp in Impel Down" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b7/Ace_and_Garp_in_Impel_Down.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20230601050849" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ace and Garp in Impel Down.png" data-image-key="Ace_and_Garp_in_Impel_Down.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b7/Ace_and_Garp_in_Impel_Down.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20230601050849"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ace_and_Garp_in_Impel_Down.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Garp visiting an imprisoned Ace.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Garp adopted <a href="/wiki/Portgas_D._Ace" title="Portgas D. Ace">Ace</a> from <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a>, who requested him to take care of his son while adding that Ace does not deserve to be treated as a criminal just because of his family ties. While Garp initially thought of adopting Ace as a preposterous idea, he eventually agreed to Roger's final wish, as the latter pointed out that after multiple confrontations, he trusted the vice admiral as much as a friend. Indeed, Garp was troubled when Ace was about to face death and claimed he had no pity for a pirate, but believed family is different. He cares about him deeply, crying for his grandson as he was about to be executed for being a pirate and desperately asking why he could not have just been a Marine. In fact, after Akainu killed Ace, Garp was more than willing to kill him in revenge, and the only reason he didn't follow through was because he was restrained by Sengoku.
</p><p>When Ace was an infant, Garp would use his vacation time to visit the village often and make funny faces to cheer him up. Despite the fact that Ace was a troubled child that would beat up anyone who insulted his father, Garp seemed amused with Ace, yet never scolded him for his actions as a part of him felt sad that the child did not fully accept Roger as his father. After Luffy, Sabo and Ace had gotten along well, Garp would sometimes visit them and train them by beating them up and destroying most of the forest in the process.
</p><p>As with Luffy, Garp had high expectations for Ace to be a strong Marine but is disappointed that he chose the life of piracy, which incidentally sent him to <a href="/wiki/Impel_Down" title="Impel Down">Impel Down</a> where they were speaking about the issue. Ace refused to acknowledge the idea that he and his younger brother could have ever been Marines, considering their fathers' restless blood in their veins.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Enemies">Enemies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D22&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Gol_D._Roger">Gol D. Roger</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D23&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Back when <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a> was alive, Garp managed to corner him numerous times.<sup id="cite_ref-Roger_32-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Roger-32">[32]</a></sup> As such, they have a long history against each other with the exception to the <a href="/wiki/Rocks_Pirates" title="Rocks Pirates">Rocks Pirates</a>. Garp was one of two Marines that Roger considered to be worth his time, the other being Sengoku.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">[33]</a></sup> Due to their countless clashes, Roger came to see Garp as much a friend as the rest of his crew.<sup id="cite_ref-adoption_&amp;_rivalry_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-adoption_&amp;_rivalry-34">[34]</a></sup> Garp too had respect for him, as he not only protected Ace but also showed signs of disappointment from Ace's decision to disregard Roger being his father. Garp also acknowledged Roger's strength, stating that although Roger was extremely reckless, this is what made him become the King of the Pirates. Garp also told Dadan that although he is a Marine, he could never come to hate Roger.
</p><p>When Roger was about to be executed after turning himself in due to his terminal illness, he made a final request to Garp. He asked Garp to take care of his unborn child, as he did not deserve to be condemned as a criminal because of his father's crimes, something they both agreed on.<sup id="cite_ref-adoption_&amp;_rivalry_34-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-adoption_&amp;_rivalry-34">[34]</a></sup> While Garp had initially wanted to make Ace into a Marine rather than a pirate like Roger, he still wanted Ace to be proud of his biological father. Though in the end, Garp had no success in this endeavor either.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Edward_Newgate">Edward Newgate</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D24&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a> respected Garp and acknowledged his strength when he addressed him by his own real name, and not "brat" unlike Crocodile, Akainu, Aokiji, Kizaru, Shanks, and many others (though Garp was more in the same age group as Whitebeard, being 4 years older than him). Garp did not let Marco pass through to get to Ace's execution platform meaning he did not care how fearsome Whitebeard could be after seeing that, which is due to not only having fought Whitebeard's rival the Pirate King but also Whitebeard himself during the <a href="/wiki/God_Valley_Incident" title="God Valley Incident">God Valley Incident</a>.
</p><p>While the two are on opposite sides, Garp shares similar views with Whitebeard. They don't believe a child should be condemned or hated because of what their parents did, nor would they hate someone simply because they were enemies with their parents. They also believe it's their duty to raise and protect the next generation.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Chinjao">Chinjao</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D25&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/Chinjao" title="Chinjao">Chinjao</a> was an infamous pirate who took deep pride in his pointed head, which Garp was determined to break. Garp and Chinjao had multiple battles in the past.<sup id="cite_ref-c719_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c719-35">[35]</a></sup> After he trained by leveling eight mountains with his fists, Garp successfully dented Chinjao's head in a confrontation, depriving the latter of the means to access all of his stored treasures. This led to Chinjao holding a grudge so strong against Garp that it extended to all of his descendants and lasted over 30 years. Chinjao lifted his grudge and forgave Garp when the latter's grandson, Luffy, punched his head hard enough to return it to its former glory.<sup id="cite_ref-vs_Chinjao_36-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vs_Chinjao-36">[36]</a></sup> Chinjao also reveals that in Garp's younger days, he was like a "demon" to pirates.<sup id="cite_ref-Demon_37-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Demon-37">[37]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Shanks">Shanks</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D26&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Garp bears a grudge against <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Shanks</a>, because Garp believes he is the one who influenced his grandson, Monkey D. Luffy, to become a pirate.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">[38]</a></sup> When seeing him at Marineford, Garp was greatly angered by his presence and deepened his grudge against Shanks for inspiring his grandson to be a pirate.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">[39]</a></sup> Despite his resentment, Garp did not stop Shanks from giving his late grandson Ace a proper burial after he requested it.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Rocks_D._Xebec">Rocks D. Xebec</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D27&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Before Roger's era, <a href="/wiki/Rocks_D._Xebec" title="Rocks D. Xebec">Rocks</a> was his enemy. There was a conflict at God Valley that required Garp to team up with Roger in order to put an end to his reign of terror.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kuzan">Kuzan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D28&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Garp is the former mentor of <a href="/wiki/Kuzan" title="Kuzan">Kuzan</a>, during their time in the Marines.<sup id="cite_ref-mentor_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-mentor-40">[40]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">[41]</a></sup> Kuzan, in particular, owes a large part of his physical strength due to Garp's training and has been indebted to Garp due to a certain incident that involved Garp saving his life, and is impressed that Garp refused several promotions.
</p><p>At <a href="/wiki/Hachinosu" title="Hachinosu">Hachinosu</a> Garp confronted his former student, who had since become a member of the <a href="/wiki/Blackbeard_Pirates" title="Blackbeard Pirates">Blackbeard Pirates</a>, he demanded Kuzan to come back to the Marines, unfreeze <a href="/wiki/Hibari" title="Hibari">Hibari</a> and let them leave with Koby. However, Kuzan rejected Garp's plea and refused to return to the Marines due to his hatred towards <a href="/wiki/Sakazuki" title="Sakazuki">Sakazuki</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c1081_42-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1081-42">[42]</a></sup> The two traded blows as they argued. Garp grew frustrated by Kuzan's stubbornness and told him that he should consider himself expelled as a pupil<sup id="cite_ref-c1087_43-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1087-43">[43]</a></sup>. The battle ended when Kuzan delivered what he thought would be a finishing blow, and pierced Garp's chest with a massive icicle. In the end Kuzan appeared dismayed because he failed to kill his former mentor.<sup id="cite_ref-c1088_18-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1088-18">[18]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_Pirates">Other Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D29&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Over his many years as a Marine hero, Garp has made many enemies with pirates over the sea, such as <a href="/wiki/Shiki" title="Shiki">Shiki</a> and <a href="/wiki/Shakuyaku" title="Shakuyaku">Shakky</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Shakuyaku_44-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Shakuyaku-44">[44]</a></sup> He felt neither remorse nor pity for any of these pirates, as they are criminals.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Others">Others</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D30&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Curly_Dadan">Curly Dadan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D31&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>It is unknown how they met, but they have known each other for at least 22 years, since Garp was seen entrusting a newborn <a href="/wiki/Portgas_D._Ace" title="Portgas D. Ace">Portgas D. Ace</a> to her.
</p><p>As <a href="/wiki/Curly_Dadan" title="Curly Dadan">Curly Dadan</a> is the leader of a <a href="/wiki/Mountain_Bandits" class="mw-redirect" title="Mountain Bandits">bandit group</a>, Garp blackmailed her to watch over Ace and Luffy as their foster mother, in exchange that he will turn a blind eye on their criminal activities, which is said to equal the numbers of stars in the sky. Despite Dadan having a fear and irritation against the vice admiral for leaving two children in her care, Garp claims that Dadan is a friend of his. This is ironic, as Garp claimed that he has no sympathy for criminals and will arrest them with ease. Even in more recent times, Garp and Dadan continue to show a violent relationship that likewise harbors respect for each other and for the work they had in connection with both Luffy and Ace.
</p><p>Even though Dadan usually fears him, she did not have a problem attacking Garp for not managing to save Ace. In turn, Garp did not resist as he understood her grief.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Sabo">Sabo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D32&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Little is known about Garp's relationship with <a href="/wiki/Sabo" title="Sabo">Sabo</a>, beyond the fact that Garp trained him along with Luffy and Ace. Sabo noted that Garp tried to keep the three brothers on a short leash, implying that he gave Sabo similar treatment to Ace and Luffy.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">[45]</a></sup> This is expanded in the anime when Luffy told Garp he, Sabo, and Ace had exchanged cups of sake. He then declared that there were three fools in need of a lesson and decided to "train" Sabo alongside Luffy and Ace.
</p>
