<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Sterry">Sterry</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D33&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>As the ruler of the <a href="/wiki/Goa_Kingdom" title="Goa Kingdom">Goa Kingdom</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sterry" title="Sterry">Sterry</a> expected absolute obedience and respect from Garp since he is one of its citizens. However, the old Marine showed neither to the young <a href="/wiki/King_(Title)" title="King (Title)">king</a>, not even knowing who he was and even telling him to get lost and calling him ugly. When he was told of Sterry's position, he only half-heartedly took back much of what he said. He even looked down on Sterry's desire to become a Celestial Dragon and bluntly expressed this aloud.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">[46]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Neptune_Family">Neptune Family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D34&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Garp became acquainted with <a href="/wiki/Neptune" title="Neptune">Neptune</a>'s family, notably Neptune and <a href="/wiki/Shirahoshi" title="Shirahoshi">Shirahoshi</a> due to being Luffy's grandfather. When they parted, Garp happily waved goodbye to the mermaid princess.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Abilities_and_Powers">Abilities and Powers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D35&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/52/Galaxy_Divide.png/revision/latest?cb=20241013020738" class="image"><img alt="Galaxy Divide" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="192" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Galaxy Divide.png" data-image-key="Galaxy_Divide.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/52/Galaxy_Divide.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20241013020738"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/52/Galaxy_Divide.png/revision/latest?cb=20241013020738" class="image"><img alt="Galaxy Divide" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/52/Galaxy_Divide.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20241013020738" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="192" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Galaxy Divide.png" data-image-key="Galaxy_Divide.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/52/Galaxy_Divide.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20241013020738"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Galaxy_Divide.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Even at an advanced age, Garp has enough raw strength and power to devastate an island.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Garp is considered a living legend and is one of the strongest Marines of all time. In his heyday he was famous for cornering <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a> many times,<sup id="cite_ref-Roger_32-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Roger-32">[32]</a></sup> as he was one of the very few people capable of fighting the Pirate King.<sup id="cite_ref-c965_47-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c965-47">[47]</a></sup> In fact, Roger states that he and Garp had almost killed each other many times throughout their battles.<sup id="cite_ref-adoption_&amp;_rivalry_34-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-adoption_&amp;_rivalry-34">[34]</a></sup> Due to his incredible power and popularity, Garp was offered the rank of <a href="/wiki/Admiral" title="Admiral">Admiral</a> several times throughout his life but refused the promotion every time.<sup id="cite_ref-AdmiralPromotion_48-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AdmiralPromotion-48">[48]</a></sup>  This is even more impressive given the fact that most admirals are shown to have powerful (mostly <a href="/wiki/Logia" title="Logia">Logia</a>-type) Devil Fruit powers. As a testament to his strength, together with Roger he fought and defeated the <a href="/wiki/Rocks_Pirates" title="Rocks Pirates">Rocks Pirates</a>, one of the strongest pirate crews in history that featured Roger's most formidable rival, <a href="/wiki/Rocks_D._Xebec" title="Rocks D. Xebec">Rocks D. Xebec</a>; three future Emperors, <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Edward Newgate</a>, <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Charlotte Linlin</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a>; and other legendary pirates such as <a href="/wiki/Shiki" title="Shiki">Shiki the Golden Lion</a>. This tremendous feat earned Garp the title of <b>"Hero of the Marines"</b>.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">[49]</a></sup> Despite his advanced age, his power and reputation are so immense that <a href="/wiki/Cross_Guild" title="Cross Guild">Cross Guild</a> has given him a bounty of <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload"></a></span> 3,000,000,000, the same bounty as an Admiral.<sup id="cite_ref-bounty_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bounty-11">[11]</a></sup>
</p><p>As another testament to his sheer power, Garp defeated and nearly killed Don <a href="/wiki/Chinjao" title="Chinjao">Chinjao</a> in the past with a single punch, whose bounty was worth <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload"></a></span>542,000,000 in his prime and was said to be able to split a continent with a headbutt, this earned him the epithet, <b>"Garp the Fist"</b>.<sup id="cite_ref-c719_35-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c719-35">[35]</a></sup> Chinjao himself said that during that time, all the pirates saw Garp as a "Devil" to them.<sup id="cite_ref-Demon_37-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Demon-37">[37]</a></sup>
</p><p>Even at the ripe age of 76, he was shown to be able to easily strike down <a href="/wiki/Marco" title="Marco">Marco the Phoenix</a>, Whitebeard's right hand, which was something that both <a href="/wiki/Borsalino" title="Borsalino">Kizaru</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sakazuki" title="Sakazuki">Akainu</a> seemed unable to do. In fact, during the War after Ace's death, Akainu would possibly have been killed by a furious Garp had <a href="/wiki/Sengoku" title="Sengoku">Sengoku</a> not restrained him. Whereas it took Akainu 10 days to barely defeat <a href="/wiki/Kuzan" title="Kuzan">Aokiji</a>, Garp was able to easily overpower the latter in moments. During the raid on Hachinosu, he battled his former student, Kuzan, and the other Titanic Captains present there—<a href="/wiki/Sanjuan_Wolf" title="Sanjuan Wolf">Sanjuan Wolf</a>, <a href="/wiki/Shiryu" title="Shiryu">Shiryu</a>, <a href="/wiki/Avalo_Pizarro" title="Avalo Pizarro">Avalo Pizarro</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Vasco_Shot" title="Vasco Shot">Vasco Shot</a>—all at once, while he initially held the upper-hand he was eventually overwhelmed after being stabbed through the abdomen by Shiryu to protect Koby. Despite this he held them off long enough to cover the Marines' escape.<sup id="cite_ref-c1088_18-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1088-18">[18]</a></sup>
</p><p>Similarly, when it was revealed worldwide that Luffy is Garp's grandson, Luffy's fame rose based on that fact, as <a href="/wiki/Demaro_Black" class="mw-redirect" title="Demaro Black">Demaro Black</a> attempted to use that as one of the strong points in his impersonation of Luffy. Charlotte Linlin referenced Garp when Luffy challenged her. He has merits and influence great enough to make even the World Nobles do not dare to get rid of him despite his rebellious personality. <a href="/wiki/Jaygarcia_Saturn" title="Jaygarcia Saturn">Jaygarcia Saturn</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Five_Elders" title="Five Elders">Five Elders</a> remarked how Luffy's record is understandable, being Garp's grandson.
</p><p>In addition, like his late rival, Gol D. Roger, Garp has never displayed any signs of being a Devil Fruit user, which makes everything he accomplished even more impressive.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Leadership">Leadership</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D36&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/33/Garp_and_SWORD_Battle_Pirates_on_Hachinosu.png/revision/latest?cb=20241006020615" class="image"><img alt="Garp and SWORD Battle Pirates on Hachinosu" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Garp and SWORD Battle Pirates on Hachinosu.png" data-image-key="Garp_and_SWORD_Battle_Pirates_on_Hachinosu.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/33/Garp_and_SWORD_Battle_Pirates_on_Hachinosu.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20241006020615"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/33/Garp_and_SWORD_Battle_Pirates_on_Hachinosu.png/revision/latest?cb=20241006020615" class="image"><img alt="Garp and SWORD Battle Pirates on Hachinosu" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/33/Garp_and_SWORD_Battle_Pirates_on_Hachinosu.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20241006020615" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Garp and SWORD Battle Pirates on Hachinosu.png" data-image-key="Garp_and_SWORD_Battle_Pirates_on_Hachinosu.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/33/Garp_and_SWORD_Battle_Pirates_on_Hachinosu.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20241006020615"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Garp_and_SWORD_Battle_Pirates_on_Hachinosu.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Garp is able to lead the elite members of <a href="/wiki/SWORD" title="SWORD">SWORD</a> against the waves of pirates on <a href="/wiki/Hachinosu" title="Hachinosu">Hachinosu</a>.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As a Vice Admiral of the <a href="/wiki/Marine_Headquarters" title="Marine Headquarters">Marine Headquarters</a>, Garp has command over all lower ranking soldiers, as seen when he took two of <a href="/wiki/Ripper" title="Ripper">Ripper</a>'s subordinates (Koby and Helmeppo) and made them his own subordinates instead due to his higher rank.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">[50]</a></sup> Also, as a Vice Admiral, he has the potential to be called upon to be one of five Vice Admirals leading a fleet of ten battleships during a <a href="/wiki/Buster_Call" title="Buster Call">Buster Call</a>.
</p><p>Being a Marine Vice Admiral and the commanding officer of the 153rd Marine Branch, Garp possesses leadership skills and is well respected by many among the Marines, having mentored many other prominent figures in the Marines, including former Admiral Kuzan.
</p><p>Garp is also a great teacher, as he was able to make Koby and Helmeppo capable fighters in a short period of time, and he was also selected to be an instructor. He was also the one who trained Luffy and Ace into being strong enough to set sail on their own. After the Summit War of Marineford, Garp now trained the new recruits of young Marines. Kuzan, who was at the time as a cadet who already learned all he could from the official instructors, was able to become the powerful warrior he is today thanks to Garp's tutelage.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_Abilities">Physical Abilities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D37&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Garp is one of the strongest Marines, whose physical strength is considered legendary, having fought many powerful pirates including the Rock Pirates and Gol D. Roger himself in his prime. At his best he had monstrous punching power at his disposal, with his epithet, <b>"Garp the Fist"</b>, attesting to the immense power of his punches. He claimed to have crushed eight mountains during his training to face Chinjao. This is proven when he was able to dent Chinjao's drill head, which was powerful enough to split the immensely hard Ice Continent in two, with relative ease. In his youth and even all the way to old age, he would use retired <a href="/wiki/Marine_Ships" title="Marine Ships">battleships</a> as punching bags, often doing so every day for years, without using Haki to build up punching power. As a result, he became capable of caving in the armored hulls of those ships with the strength of his fists alone.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">[51]</a></sup> It is evident <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a> respects Garp's strength, as he mentioned him during his talk with <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Shanks</a>.
</p><p>Even in old age, Garp still remains powerful, being able to launch iron cannonballs like baseballs at higher velocities than if they were fired from a real cannon, break through brick walls and cannon supports with his fists and carry and throw a giant iron ball and chain many times bigger than the Thousand Sunny. During the Summit War of Marineford, he struck down and injured a <a href="/wiki/Tori_Tori_no_Mi,_Model:_Phoenix" title="Tori Tori no Mi, Model: Phoenix">Mythical Zoan</a> user like <a href="/wiki/Marco" title="Marco">Marco</a> with a single blow and, in the anime, Garp took down <a href="/wiki/Jesus_Burgess" title="Jesus Burgess">Jesus Burgess</a>, a master fighter with titanic physical strength effortlessly. In conjunction with his tremendous mastery of Haki, Garp's strength becomes monstrous, as he was able to obliterate a portion of a town with a single blow, toss <a href="/wiki/Sanjuan_Wolf" title="Sanjuan Wolf">Sanjuan Wolf</a>, a giant with the ability to <a href="/wiki/Deka_Deka_no_Mi" title="Deka Deka no Mi">grow even more enormous</a> clean into the ocean and almost drowned him in the process, and decimate multiple structures and land masses connected to <a href="/wiki/Avalo_Pizarro" title="Avalo Pizarro">Avalo Pizarro</a> and his <a href="/wiki/Shima_Shima_no_Mi" title="Shima Shima no Mi">Devil Fruit</a>.
</p><p>In addition to his immense physical strength, Garp also has tremendous levels of durability and tolerance to pain, as seen when his chest was deeply slashed by Captain <a href="/wiki/Morgan" title="Morgan">Morgan</a>'s axe hand, only to recover mere seconds later, with no obvious pain and apparently oblivious to the fact that he was struck at all. In fact, when informed by one of the Marines that he was nearly killed, he mistook this for one of the men being killed. It was only when he saw what the wound did, he realized what happened, as he fell asleep before being attacked. He was able to get back on his feet after allowing himself to be punched by Luffy in <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_2_Techniques" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 2 Techniques">Gear 2</a> at point-blank range without losing consciousness and was still able to fight the <a href="/wiki/Blackbeard_Pirates" title="Blackbeard Pirates">Blackbeard Pirates</a> along with <a href="/wiki/Sengoku" title="Sengoku">Sengoku</a>. On Hachinosu, Garp took numerous attacks from <a href="/wiki/Kuzan" title="Kuzan">Kuzan</a>, his former student who went through the same battleship punching training as Garp and came out with noticeably very little damage from his punches or his <a href="/wiki/Hie_Hie_no_Mi" title="Hie Hie no Mi">ice-based</a> attacks. He was also run through with a sword by <a href="/wiki/Shiryu" title="Shiryu">Shiryu</a>, but not only did he shrug off the injury and attack Shiryu, but continued to fight a large number of the pirates on the island, including Kuzan and the rest of the Captains of the Blackbeard Pirates, holding them off long enough for the marines and the all the people rescued from the island to successfully escape.<sup id="cite_ref-c1087_43-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1087-43">[43]</a></sup> Even after getting overwhelmed and Kuzan going for a killer blow, Garp still survived.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">[52]</a></sup>
</p><p>Garp is also extremely fast and agile, seemingly disappearing as soon as he starts moving. He managed to bypass all of the Straw Hats in order to get to a sleeping Luffy, with none of them even being able to react until he was already past them. He is also fast enough to grab Kuzan, a former Marine Admiral, by the face and slam him to the ground before he managed to defend himself. He was quick enough to grab two random pirates just to block a flaming attack from <a href="/wiki/Vasco_Shot" title="Vasco Shot">Vasco Shot</a>, and even after being stabbed by Shiryu, was able to move around fast enough to bowl over Kuzan and travel across the island to land a devastating attack on Avalo Pizarro.<sup id="cite_ref-c1088_18-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1088-18">[18]</a></sup> 
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Techniques">Techniques</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D38&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b9/Galaxy_Impact.png/revision/latest?cb=20240814162313" class="image"><img alt="Galaxy Impact" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="237" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Galaxy Impact.png" data-image-key="Galaxy_Impact.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b9/Galaxy_Impact.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814162313"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b9/Galaxy_Impact.png/revision/latest?cb=20240814162313" class="image"><img alt="Galaxy Impact" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b9/Galaxy_Impact.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814162313" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="237" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Galaxy Impact.png" data-image-key="Galaxy_Impact.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b9/Galaxy_Impact.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814162313"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Galaxy_Impact.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Garp uses "Galaxy Impact", a powerful Supreme King Haki-infused attack.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b>Ai aru Kobushi</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">愛ある拳</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, literally meaning "Fist of Love")</span>: A gag technique. It is a simple but powerful punch used to strike Luffy on his head. Garp had been shown to have used this on Ace during his childhood as well. In <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece:_Pirate_Warriors_2" title="One Piece: Pirate Warriors 2">Pirate Warriors 2</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece:_Pirate_Warriors_3" title="One Piece: Pirate Warriors 3">Pirate Warriors 3</a></i>, the game adds the visual effect of a giant fist coming down on the enemies and is Garp's first Special Attack in both games. In the Funimation adaptions, it is called <b>Fist of Love</b>.</li>
<li><b>Galaxy Impact</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja"><ruby lang="ja"><rb>拳骨衝突</rb><rp>（</rp><rt>ギャラクシーインパクト</rt><rp>）</rp></ruby></span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Gyarakushī Inpakuto</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, literally meaning "Fist Collision")</span>: Garp infuses his fist with advanced <a href="/wiki/Haki/Armament_Haki" title="Haki/Armament Haki">Armament Haki</a> and <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a> and then delivers a massively powerful shockwave punch that surrounds an enormous radius, devastating anything in its range. This attack was first seen used against the <a href="/wiki/Blackbeard_Pirates" title="Blackbeard Pirates">Blackbeard Pirates</a> on <a href="/wiki/Hachinosu" title="Hachinosu">Hachinosu</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c1080_53-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1080-53">[53]</a></sup> In the anime, the shockwave looks more like an enormous explosion; in addition, while charging the attack, Garp's fist generates a massive red flash of light.
<ul><li><b>Galaxy Divide</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja"><ruby lang="ja"><rb>拳骨唐竹割</rb><rp>（</rp><rt>ギャラクシーディバイド</rt><rp>）</rp></ruby></span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Gyarakushī Dibaido</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, literally meaning "Fist Cleaving")</span>: Garp infuses his fist with Armament and Supreme King Haki and then delivers a powerful shockwave punch that creates a vertical fissure on his target. This was first seen used against the Hachinosu skull face <a href="/wiki/Shima_Shima_no_Mi" title="Shima Shima no Mi">controlled</a> by <a href="/wiki/Avalo_Pizarro" title="Avalo Pizarro">Avalo Pizarro</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c1088p10-11_54-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1088p10-11-54">[54]</a></sup> The name of the technique references a <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/kenjutsu" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:kenjutsu">kenjutsu</a></i> technique called <i>karatake wari</i><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">唐竹割り</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, "splitting the Chinese bamboo")</span>, a downward vertical cut.</li></ul></li>
<li><b>Blue Hole</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja"><ruby lang="ja"><rb>海底落下</rb><rp>（</rp><rt>ブルーホール</rt><rp>）</rp></ruby></span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Burū Hōru</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, literally meaning "Seafloor Fall")</span>: After hardening his hand with Armament Haki and infusing it with Supreme King Haki, Garp grabs an opponent by the face and slams them downwards, creating a massively deep hole in the ground as they fall. This was first seen used against <a href="/wiki/Kuzan" title="Kuzan">Kuzan</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c1081_42-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1081-42">[42]</a></sup> A <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/blue_hole" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:blue hole">blue hole</a> is a large marine cavern or sinkhole.</li>
<li><b>Kaizoku Hinotama</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">海賊火の玉</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, literally meaning "Pirate Fireballs")</span>: An improvised technique Garp came up with after he used the bodies of defeated pirates to shield himself from <a href="/wiki/Vasco_Shot" title="Vasco Shot">Vasco Shot</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Gabu_Gabu_no_Mi#Techniques" title="Gabu Gabu no Mi">fire stream</a>. After the attack resulted in the pirates being engulfed in flames, Garp threw them in various directions causing damage to other pirates surrounding him.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">[55]</a></sup> In the VIZ manga, this is called <b>Pirate Fireballs</b>.</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Rokushiki">Rokushiki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D39&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article: <a href="/wiki/Rokushiki" title="Rokushiki">Rokushiki</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>Garp is seemingly able to use <a href="/wiki/Rokushiki/Soru" title="Rokushiki/Soru">Soru</a> to move at great speed, being able to close the distance between himself and Kuzan in an instant.<sup id="cite_ref-c1081_42-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1081-42">[42]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Haki">Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D40&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article: <a href="/wiki/Haki" title="Haki">Haki</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>As a Vice Admiral of the Marines, Garp is fully capable of using Haki.<sup id="cite_ref-vicehaki_56-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vicehaki-56">[56]</a></sup> and is one of the very few people in the world who can use all three types of Haki. He is also a capable teacher, as he taught Kuzan, Koby and Helmeppo.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Supreme_King_Haki">Supreme King Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D41&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Garp possesses immense mastery in the usage of <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a>, a rare form of Haki that only one in several million people in the world can use.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_6-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-6">[6]</a></sup> Most notably, he is among the small "handful" of users who are capable of using the advanced application of "infusing" his Supreme King Haki into parts of his body or objects, as signified by the thin streams of black lightning emanating from his fist.<sup id="cite_ref-c1080_53-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1080-53">[53]</a></sup> Garp can also use Supreme King Haki defensively, protecting himself from the deep-freezing effects of Kuzan's <i>Ice Ball</i> before easily breaking out of it.<sup id="cite_ref-c1081_42-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1081-42">[42]</a></sup> Garp displayed advanced application at multiple points, notably during his fight with Kuzan, grabbing him by the face and sending him downward creating a large hole with a powerful Supreme King attack, and once more on <a href="/wiki/Avalo_Pizarro" title="Avalo Pizarro">Avalo Pizarro</a>, delivering a powerful Supreme King shockwave punch that left a vertical injury on the pirate.<sup id="cite_ref-c1088p10-11_54-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1088p10-11-54">[54]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Armament_Haki">Armament Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D42&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/40/Garp_vs._Chinjao.png/revision/latest?cb=20230407002858" class="image"><img alt="Garp vs" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="128" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Garp vs. Chinjao.png" data-image-key="Garp_vs._Chinjao.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/40/Garp_vs._Chinjao.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230407002858"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/40/Garp_vs._Chinjao.png/revision/latest?cb=20230407002858" class="image"><img alt="Garp vs" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/40/Garp_vs._Chinjao.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230407002858" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="128" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Garp vs. Chinjao.png" data-image-key="Garp_vs._Chinjao.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/40/Garp_vs._Chinjao.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230407002858"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Garp_vs._Chinjao.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Garp uses Armament Haki to flatten Chinjao's head.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Garp is an immensely skilled and powerful master of <a href="/wiki/Haki/Armament_Haki" title="Haki/Armament Haki">Armament Haki</a>. By hardening his fist, Garp became able to counter and even crush <a href="/wiki/Chinjao" title="Chinjao">Chinjao</a>'s Armament Haki-enhanced drill-shaped head 30 years ago, proving his superior mastery compared to Chinjao, who himself is a masterful Armament Haki user in his own right.<sup id="cite_ref-vs_Chinjao_36-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vs_Chinjao-36">[36]</a></sup> During the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">Summit War of Marineford</a>, he managed to punch and hurt <a href="/wiki/Marco" title="Marco">Marco</a>, despite the latter being in his regenerative phoenix form.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">[57]</a></sup> He can also utilize the advanced application of emitting Armament Haki out from his hands, allowing him to attack opponents without making physical contact.<sup id="cite_ref-c1080_53-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1080-53">[53]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c1081_42-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1081-42">[42]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c1088p10-11_54-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1088p10-11-54">[54]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Observation_Haki">Observation Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D43&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Garp is an extremely skilled and experienced user of <a href="/wiki/Haki/Observation_Haki" title="Haki/Observation Haki">Observation Haki</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-vicehaki_56-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vicehaki-56">[56]</a></sup> He could sense that Kuzan was present on <a href="/wiki/Hachinosu" title="Hachinosu">Hachinosu</a> and was going to freeze <a href="/wiki/Hibari" title="Hibari">Hibari</a> where other Observation Haki users (including herself, <a href="/wiki/Tashigi" title="Tashigi">Tashigi</a> and the rest of <a href="/wiki/SWORD" title="SWORD">SWORD</a>) could not sense him.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">[58]</a></sup> He was able to sense and catch Shiryu's attack when he attempted to attack a distracted Koby, despite the former jailer being <a href="/wiki/Suke_Suke_no_Mi" title="Suke Suke no Mi">invisible</a>.
</p><p>When Koby awakened Observation Haki, Dr. <a href="/wiki/Fishbonen" title="Fishbonen">Fishbonen</a> recommended that he ask Garp how to master it, suggesting Garp has enough expertise in it to mentor others.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Weapons">Weapons</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D44&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3d/Garp_Iron_Ball.png/revision/latest?cb=20200114135033" class="image"><img alt="Garp Iron Ball" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Garp Iron Ball.png" data-image-key="Garp_Iron_Ball.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3d/Garp_Iron_Ball.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20200114135033"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3d/Garp_Iron_Ball.png/revision/latest?cb=20200114135033" class="image"><img alt="Garp Iron Ball" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3d/Garp_Iron_Ball.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20200114135033" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Garp Iron Ball.png" data-image-key="Garp_Iron_Ball.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3d/Garp_Iron_Ball.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20200114135033"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Garp_Iron_Ball.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Garp preparing to throw a giant iron ball.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Garp throws cannonballs with his bare hands. The cannonballs soar much faster than when fired from a cannon, due to Garp's immense physical strength.<sup id="cite_ref-c438p11_24-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c438p11-24">[24]</a></sup> He also wields a giant iron ball, mounted on a chain, which dwarfs the size of his own Marine battleship.<sup id="cite_ref-c439_59-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c439-59">[59]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Techniques_2">Techniques</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D45&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><b>Genkotsu Meteor</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">拳骨<ruby lang="ja"><rb>隕石</rb><rp>（</rp><rt>メテオ</rt><rp>）</rp></ruby></span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Genkotsu Meteo</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, literally meaning "Fist Meteorite")</span>: Garp throws a cannonball at an enemy ship. Due to Garp's superhuman strength, he can throw them like baseballs, and the impacts are more powerful than when being fired from an actual cannon.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">[60]</a></sup> In the VIZ manga and <a href="/wiki/Funimation" title="Funimation">Funimation</a> adaptions, this is called <b>Meteor Fist</b>.</li>
<li><b>Genkotsu Ryuseigun</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">拳骨流星群</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Genkotsu Ryūseigun</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, literally meaning "Fist Meteor Swarm")</span>: Garp throws one thousand iron cannonballs at enemy ships. The cannonballs are supplied by conveyor belts on either side of him.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">[61]</a></sup> In the VIZ manga and Funimation adaptions, this is called <b>Meteor Fist Shower</b>.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Video_Game_Attacks">Video Game Attacks</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D46&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><b>Genkotsu Satellite</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">拳・骨・<ruby lang="ja"><rb>衛星</rb><rp>（</rp><rt>サテライト</rt><rp>）</rp></ruby></span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Genkotsu Sateraito</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, literally meaning "Fist Satellite")</span>: Garp throws a large cannonball at his opponent. The size of the cannonball is slightly larger than his upper body. The attack first appeared in <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece:_Pirate_Warriors_2" title="One Piece: Pirate Warriors 2">Pirate Warriors 2</a></i> as Garp's third Unique Action and is also usable in <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece:_Pirate_Warriors_3" title="One Piece: Pirate Warriors 3">Pirate Warriors 3</a></i>. In the English version it is translated as <b>Satellite Fist</b>.<sup id="cite_ref-pw2_62-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pw2-62">[62]</a></sup> The literal kanji reading for satellite is <i>eisei</i>.</li>
<li><b>Tokudai Tekkyu</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">特大鉄球</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Tokudai Tekkyū</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, literally meaning "Extra-large Iron Ball")</span>: Garp throws an enormous cannonball at his enemies. The cannonball is several times larger than his body, and its name comes from what the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hats</a> screamed when Garp threw his ship-sized cannonball at the <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Thousand Sunny</a> just before they escaped from <a href="/wiki/Water_7" title="Water 7">Water 7</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c439_59-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c439-59">[59]</a></sup> The attack is usable in <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece:_Pirate_Warriors_3" title="One Piece: Pirate Warriors 3">Pirate Warriors 3</a></i> as Garp's Special Kizuna Attack. In the English version it is translated as <b>Oversized Iron Ball</b>.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">[63]</a></sup></li>
<li><b>Cho Tokudai Tekkyu</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">超・特大鉄球</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Chō Tokudai Tekkyu</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, literally meaning "Super Extra-large Iron Ball")</span>: A slightly larger version of <b>Tokudai Tekkyu</b>. The attack first appeared in <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece:_Pirate_Warriors_2" title="One Piece: Pirate Warriors 2">Pirate Warriors 2</a></i> as Garp's second Special Attack and is also usable in <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece:_Pirate_Warriors_3" title="One Piece: Pirate Warriors 3">Pirate Warriors 3</a></i>. In the English version it is translated as <b>Super Oversized Iron Ball</b>.<sup id="cite_ref-pw2_62-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pw2-62">[62]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D47&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Past">Past</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D48&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Before_the_Great_Age_of_Pirates">Before the Great Age of Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D49&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Monkey D. Garp was born 78 years ago in the <a href="/wiki/Goa_Kingdom" title="Goa Kingdom">Goa Kingdom</a> in the <a href="/wiki/East_Blue" title="East Blue">East Blue</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_6-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-6">[6]</a></sup> He joined the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a> 56 years ago at the age of 22 along with <a href="/wiki/Tsuru" title="Tsuru">Tsuru</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sengoku" title="Sengoku">Sengoku</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">[64]</a></sup> At 23, Garp started a family with an unknown woman and had a son named <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Dragon" title="Monkey D. Dragon">Monkey D. Dragon</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">[65]</a></sup> Over the years, Garp would rise up through the ranks of the Marines, eventually achieving the rank of  <a href="/wiki/Vice_Admiral" title="Vice Admiral">Vice Admiral</a>.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/72/Marines_Arrive_At_God_Valley.png/revision/latest?cb=20231029151438" class="image"><img alt="Marines Arrive At God Valley" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="177" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Marines Arrive At God Valley.png" data-image-key="Marines_Arrive_At_God_Valley.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/72/Marines_Arrive_At_God_Valley.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231029151438"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/72/Marines_Arrive_At_God_Valley.png/revision/latest?cb=20231029151438" class="image"><img alt="Marines Arrive At God Valley" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/72/Marines_Arrive_At_God_Valley.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231029151438" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="177" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Marines Arrive At God Valley.png" data-image-key="Marines_Arrive_At_God_Valley.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/72/Marines_Arrive_At_God_Valley.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231029151438"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Marines_Arrive_At_God_Valley.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Marine forces, led by Garp, arrive at God Valley.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>38 years ago, <a href="/wiki/Kong" title="Kong">Kong</a> alerted Garp, who was on vacation, of an incident on <a href="/wiki/God_Valley" title="God Valley">God Valley</a> involving the <a href="/wiki/World_Noble" title="World Noble">World Nobles</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Rocks_Pirates" title="Rocks Pirates">Rocks Pirates</a>. Initially Garp brushed it off as the <a href="/wiki/God%27s_Knights" title="God's Knights">God's Knights</a> and other Marines were already on the island for their protection until Kong told him that the <a href="/wiki/Roger_Pirates" title="Roger Pirates">Roger Pirates</a> were also there. This revelation caused Garp to immediately take the threat seriously and head over to God Valley, bringing along <a href="/wiki/Bogard" title="Bogard">Bogard</a> and a few more Marines with him to confront <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c1096_66-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1096-66">[66]</a></sup> This event would later be labeled as the <a href="/wiki/God_Valley_Incident" title="God Valley Incident">God Valley Incident</a>, where Garp would earn his epithet of "Hero of the Marines" after successfully defeating <a href="/wiki/Rocks_D._Xebec" title="Rocks D. Xebec">Rocks D. Xebec</a> at God Valley and protecting the Nobles through joint forces with Roger, the latter a detail that was not publicly reported due to <a href="/wiki/Morgans" title="Morgans">Morgans</a> covering only Garp's heroism. Garp rarely discusses the God Valley Incident as he feels shame about this event.<sup id="cite_ref-c907_31-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c907-31">[31]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">[67]</a></sup> Around this time, Garp also chased other pirates like <a href="/wiki/Shakuyaku" title="Shakuyaku">Shakuyaku</a> as part of his duties.<sup id="cite_ref-Shakuyaku_44-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Shakuyaku-44">[44]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">[68]</a></sup> 
</p><p>At some point, Garp was approached by <a href="/wiki/Kuzan" title="Kuzan">Kuzan</a>, who had already surpassed the standard Marine training and was ready for the next level, so he asked Garp to take him on as an apprentice. Garp initially refused, but eventually, through unknown events Garp did indeed end up training Kuzan. They trained using "punching ships", the same thing as punching bags, only they trained by punching the bow of scraped ships, leaving large indents in the ships they practiced on. As a rule of the training, they were not allowed to use Haki or Devil Fruit powers, just raw brute strength. During this training, Garp became more casual with Kuzan even talking to him about his <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Dragon" title="Monkey D. Dragon">son</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-mentor_40-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-mentor-40">[40]</a></sup>
</p><p>Thirty years ago, he fought <a href="/wiki/Chinjao" title="Chinjao">Chinjao</a> and got his epithet as "Garp the Fist"<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_6-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-6">[6]</a></sup> and also earned his hatred after denting his pointy head, which was the strongest head of that time, and robbing him of the means to acquire the treasure from the Ice Continent.<sup id="cite_ref-vs_Chinjao_36-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vs_Chinjao-36">[36]</a></sup> He became famous for cornering and fighting the late Pirate King, <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a>, numerous times in his career. Garp was offered a promotion to admiral position many times from Fleet Admiral Kong, but he declined every time. The main reason was because he refused to work under authority of the Celestial Dragons, according to Sengoku's statement.<sup id="cite_ref-c957p9_26-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c957p9-26">[26]</a></sup>
</p><p>Three years before Roger's execution, Garp hears about the Roger Pirates and the <a href="/wiki/Golden_Lion_Pirates" title="Golden Lion Pirates">Golden Lion Pirates</a> confrontation at <a href="/wiki/Edd_War" title="Edd War">Edd War</a>. He then walks out on the then <a href="/wiki/Marine_Ranks#Fleet_Admiral" title="Marine Ranks">Fleet Admiral</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kong" title="Kong">Kong</a>'s office, and was accompanied by Tsuru, <a href="/wiki/Jaguar_D._Saul" title="Jaguar D. Saul">Jaguar D. Saul</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sakazuki" title="Sakazuki">Sakazuki</a> and Kuzan who remarked that he rejected another promotion with Garp rebuffing it and asked Tsuru to give her ship to him. He then forces his way onto <a href="/wiki/Admiral" title="Admiral">Admiral</a> <a href="/wiki/Sengoku" title="Sengoku">Sengoku</a>'s ship, much to Sengoku's annoyance.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">[69]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/92/Roger_Asks_Garp_to_Protect_Ace.png/revision/latest?cb=20230716184356" class="image"><img alt="Roger Asks Garp to Protect Ace" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Roger Asks Garp to Protect Ace.png" data-image-key="Roger_Asks_Garp_to_Protect_Ace.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/92/Roger_Asks_Garp_to_Protect_Ace.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230716184356"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/92/Roger_Asks_Garp_to_Protect_Ace.png/revision/latest?cb=20230716184356" class="image"><img alt="Roger Asks Garp to Protect Ace" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/92/Roger_Asks_Garp_to_Protect_Ace.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230716184356" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Roger Asks Garp to Protect Ace.png" data-image-key="Roger_Asks_Garp_to_Protect_Ace.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/92/Roger_Asks_Garp_to_Protect_Ace.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230716184356"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Roger_Asks_Garp_to_Protect_Ace.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Roger asking Garp to protect his child.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Prior to Roger's execution, the Pirate King requested Garp to take care of his then-unborn child, as he thought the child did not deserve to be branded a criminal due to being born to a pirate.<sup id="cite_ref-adoption_&amp;_rivalry_34-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-adoption_&amp;_rivalry-34">[34]</a></sup>
</p><p>When <a href="/wiki/Shiki" title="Shiki">Shiki the Golden Lion</a> attacked <a href="/wiki/Marineford" title="Marineford">Marineford</a> a week before Roger's execution, Garp and Sengoku challenged him together. After a grueling battle that devastated half of Marineford, they managed to defeat him. A number of months after the Pirate King's death, Garp went to <a href="/wiki/Baterilla" title="Baterilla">Baterilla</a> and visited <a href="/wiki/Portgas_D._Rouge" title="Portgas D. Rouge">Portgas D. Rouge</a>. He was present at Ace's birth and Rouge's death afterward. Honoring Roger's last request, Garp took Ace to <a href="/wiki/Dawn_Island" title="Dawn Island">Dawn Island</a> to be raised by <a href="/wiki/Curly_Dadan" title="Curly Dadan">Dadan</a>. Garp would visit Ace during his vacations. Seventeen years prior to the start of the story, Garp became a grandfather to a newly born <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> after his <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Dragon" title="Monkey D. Dragon">son</a> had left him in his care.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="The_Three_Brothers">The Three Brothers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D50&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/58/Garp_Delivers_Luffy.png/revision/latest?cb=20231203012834" class="image"><img alt="Garp Delivers Luffy" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="157" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Garp Delivers Luffy.png" data-image-key="Garp_Delivers_Luffy.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/58/Garp_Delivers_Luffy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231203012834"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/58/Garp_Delivers_Luffy.png/revision/latest?cb=20231203012834" class="image"><img alt="Garp Delivers Luffy" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/58/Garp_Delivers_Luffy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231203012834" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="157" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Garp Delivers Luffy.png" data-image-key="Garp_Delivers_Luffy.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/58/Garp_Delivers_Luffy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231203012834"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Garp_Delivers_Luffy.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Garp sending Luffy to live with Dadan.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Early on in Luffy's life, Garp trained him to become a strong Marine. Luffy was thrown into valleys, left alone in dangerous forests, and tied to balloons over high altitudes, all for the sake of making him stronger. After this, he left Luffy in the care of Dadan.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">[70]</a></sup> Despite Dadan not wanting to take care of another one of Garp's children, she complied. When Dadan voiced her displeasure of Garp's irresponsibility to take care of them himself, he became angered, making Dadan immediately take back what she said.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">[71]</a></sup>
</p><p>Throughout his visits, he would often hold "training sessions" with Luffy and Ace and on one occasion with <a href="/wiki/Sabo" title="Sabo">Sabo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">[72]</a></sup> When Garp first read in the <a href="/wiki/Newspaper" title="Newspaper">newspaper</a> that Ace had become the captain of the <a href="/wiki/Spade_Pirates" title="Spade Pirates">Spade Pirates</a>, he was furious.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">[73]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Diary_of_Koby-Meppo">Diary of Koby-Meppo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D51&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Garp was first introduced as the Marine Officer in charge of escorting Captain <a href="/wiki/Morgan" title="Morgan">Morgan</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">[74]</a></sup> However, after Garp fell asleep, Morgan made his escape by striking Garp and taking <a href="/wiki/Helmeppo" title="Helmeppo">Helmeppo</a> as a hostage, fleeing on a small boat. Garp then woke up unfazed and broke a cannon while waking up.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">[75]</a></sup>
</p><p>After Koby returned with Helmeppo, they offered themselves to be punished, but Garp decided to take charge of the pair. He took them back to <a href="/wiki/Marine_Headquarters" title="Marine Headquarters">Marine Headquarters</a> and oversaw their training.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">[76]</a></sup> During a class, Garp asked the recruits what they would do if they were riding in a boat and could only bring either a baby or an old man onboard. When Koby answered that he would let both of them ride in the boat instead of himself, Garp threw a marker at him and told him that answer was wrong, explaining that the baby should be saved because the old man would not have much time left to live. He added that the most important thing that the Marines should be trying to protect is the future of the people, meaning that the survival of babies and young people like Koby are more important than that of an old man. <a href="/wiki/Hototogisu" title="Hototogisu">Hototogisu</a> later hit Garp over the head with a bat and scolded him for his lecture, explaining that all lives mattered, but Garp insisted that the future of the young people was limitless.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">[77]</a></sup> When Garp questioned Helmeppo about Koby's bandaged hands, Helmeppo explained that every night after their training with Garp, Koby would practice punching battleship bags to further hone his strength.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">[78]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="Jango.27s_Dance_Paradise"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Jango's_Dance_Paradise">Jango's Dance Paradise</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D52&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>He appears walking alongside Koby and Helmeppo, showing some of their physical change during Garp's training.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">[79]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Water_7_Saga">Water 7 Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D53&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Post-Enies_Lobby_Arc">Post-Enies Lobby Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D54&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After arriving at <a href="/wiki/Water_7" title="Water 7">Water 7</a>, he went to the small house where Luffy was recuperating from his battles at <a href="/wiki/Enies_Lobby" title="Enies Lobby">Enies Lobby</a>. Vice Admiral Garp marched to the front of the temporary <a href="/wiki/Galley-La_Headquarters" title="Galley-La Headquarters">Galley-La Headquarters</a> and told two subordinates in specific to wait outside. Garp broke through the wall and into the Straw Hats' room. He asked if they were the Straw Hats as everyone prepared to fight, but before they could do anything, Garp passed them and punched a sleeping Luffy's head into the floor, telling him to wake up. To everyone's surprise, Luffy screamed in pain. Garp then said that no one can escape his Fist of Love. He then removed his mask and told Luffy he heard he had been doing reckless things. Luffy was shocked to see that the man behind the mask was none other than his grandfather, and everyone else were even more surprised that Luffy's grandfather is a high-ranking Marine.<sup id="cite_ref-Grandfather_14-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Grandfather-14">[14]</a></sup>
</p><p>Garp said Luffy owed him an apology as he was causing trouble. Luffy told the others not to fight with his grandfather, as Garp had nearly killed him on many occasions in his childhood. Garp snapped at Luffy for making him sound like a bad guy for what he did in the past and claimed those incidents were aimed at turning Luffy into a strong man.
</p><p>Garp reminded Luffy that he wanted him to be a strong Marine, which Luffy countered by claiming he had always told him he wanted to be a pirate. Garp responded by saying that Luffy was negatively influenced by Shanks, to which Luffy took offense because Shanks saved his life. Garp suddenly grabbed Luffy, asking if he was trying to tell his grandpa what to do. Luffy's crew panicked over what to do until they found the pair have fallen asleep. Garp, being the first of the two to wake up, punched Luffy awake for falling asleep on him, while the others pointed out Garp did the same. Garp then ordered his men to repair the wall he damaged. The men said that Garp should help repair the wall as he destroyed it. Garp explained he did so because he thought it would look cool.
</p><p>As Garp repaired the wall, he said he heard that Luffy met his father at <a href="/wiki/Loguetown" title="Loguetown">Loguetown</a>. Luffy did not have a clue about it and was clueless of even having a father in the first place. Garp then announced that Luffy's father is the revolutionary <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Dragon" title="Monkey D. Dragon">Monkey D. Dragon</a>, causing a sudden shock amongst all those around him. After Robin explained to Luffy about Dragon, the <a href="/wiki/Revolutionary_Army" title="Revolutionary Army">Revolutionary Army</a>, and their goals, Garp turned around and said that he should not have said that, asking them to forget he said anything, causing even more shock amongst everyone.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">[80]</a></sup>
</p><p>Garp told Luffy that he would let him go since he is his grandson and would use that as an excuse when informing his superior officers. However, his advisor <a href="/wiki/Bogard" title="Bogard">Bogard</a> told Garp it would be better to lie and say the Straw Hats got away. Garp then said that he mostly came for his students and announced his departure. Luffy said goodbye and Garp punched him, saying he was letting him leave too easily and berated him for being too casual about saying goodbye to his grandfather whom he had not seen in a while. Luffy complained by saying the only thing Garp has ever done was hit him to which Garp replied he just wanted to show love to and be loved by his grandson.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">[81]</a></sup>
</p><p>Some days later, Fleet Admiral <a href="/wiki/Sengoku" title="Sengoku">Sengoku</a> ordered Garp to return to Water 7 to capture Luffy. Garp's ship picked up <a href="/wiki/Kuzan" title="Kuzan">Aokiji</a> along the way, but only because he did not want to ride his bicycle. After returning to Water 7, Garp announced to Luffy that he was going to die there. Luffy argued that he said he would not attack, but Garp simply said he got his orders and proceeded to attack by throwing a cannonball at breakneck speed at them. The Straw Hats were amazed but prepared to defend the ship and started to set sail. Garp then asked for one thousand cannonballs, intending to throw them all at them. Garp began to get flustered and threw another cannonball, but Luffy knocked it out of the way. Luffy said he really had to run and hoped they would see each other again sometime.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">[82]</a></sup>
</p><p>Garp then took out an enormous iron ball and tossed it at the <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Thousand Sunny</a>. Before it could crush the Thousand Sunny, <a href="/wiki/Franky" title="Franky">Franky</a> activated Coup de Burst to launch the ship up into the sky. The Straw Hats got away, but Garp just laughed.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">[83]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Summit_War_Saga">Summit War Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D55&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><small>
</small></p><small><hr></small><small></small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>The following events are <a href="/wiki/Canon#Non-Canon" title="Canon">Non-Canon</a> and therefore not considered part of the <a href="/wiki/Canon" title="Canon">Canon</a> story.</b></i></span>
</p><small><hr></small>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="One_Piece_Film:_Strong_World">One Piece Film: Strong World</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D56&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a5/Garp_Recognizes_Shiki%27s_Ability.png/revision/latest?cb=20230731225351" class="image"><img alt="Garp Recognizes Shiki's Ability" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Garp Recognizes Shiki's Ability.png" data-image-key="Garp_Recognizes_Shiki%27s_Ability.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a5/Garp_Recognizes_Shiki%27s_Ability.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230731225351"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a5/Garp_Recognizes_Shiki%27s_Ability.png/revision/latest?cb=20230731225351" class="image"><img alt="Garp Recognizes Shiki's Ability" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a5/Garp_Recognizes_Shiki%27s_Ability.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230731225351" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Garp Recognizes Shiki's Ability.png" data-image-key="Garp_Recognizes_Shiki%27s_Ability.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a5/Garp_Recognizes_Shiki%27s_Ability.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230731225351"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Garp_Recognizes_Shiki%27s_Ability.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Garp during Shiki's attack on Marineford Headquarters.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When <a href="/wiki/Shiki" title="Shiki">Shiki</a> returned from his 20-year disappearance, he attacked Marineford Headquarters by using his <a href="/wiki/Fuwa_Fuwa_no_Mi" title="Fuwa Fuwa no Mi">powers to levitate</a> and hurl fleets of ships at the island. Garp identified Shiki right away, recognizing his abilities from past encounters. Garp wondered if he had returned to get revenge on the world.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">[84]</a></sup>
<small>
</small></p><small><hr></small><small></small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>Concludes non-canon section.</b></i></span>
</p><small><hr></small>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Sabaody_Archipelago_Arc">Sabaody Archipelago Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D57&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After his grandson's assault on <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark" title="Thriller Bark">Thriller Bark</a>, he was seen at <a href="/wiki/Mary_Geoise" title="Mary Geoise">Mary Geoise</a> with <a href="/wiki/Bartholomew_Kuma" title="Bartholomew Kuma">Bartholomew Kuma</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sengoku" title="Sengoku">Sengoku</a>, where he laughed at how Luffy had avoided capture by Kuma and annoyed Sengoku by talking about tea and crackers.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">[85]</a></sup>
</p><p>Recently, Garp found out that <a href="/wiki/Silvers_Rayleigh" title="Silvers Rayleigh">Silvers Rayleigh</a> was to be sold as a <a href="/wiki/Slavery" title="Slavery">slave</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Sabaody_Archipelago" title="Sabaody Archipelago">Sabaody Archipelago</a>, whom he assumed let himself get captured to pay off a gambling debt. Due to the Marines being busy with the incident regarding <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a> and the execution of <a href="/wiki/Portgas_D._Ace" title="Portgas D. Ace">Portgas D. Ace</a>, Garp remarked that he would take care of the situation.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">[86]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Impel_Down_Arc">Impel Down Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D58&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
