<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f9/Garp_and_Sengoku.png/revision/latest?cb=20230507213433" class="image"><img alt="Garp and Sengoku" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Garp and Sengoku.png" data-image-key="Garp_and_Sengoku.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f9/Garp_and_Sengoku.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230507213433"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f9/Garp_and_Sengoku.png/revision/latest?cb=20230507213433" class="image"><img alt="Garp and Sengoku" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f9/Garp_and_Sengoku.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230507213433" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Garp and Sengoku.png" data-image-key="Garp_and_Sengoku.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f9/Garp_and_Sengoku.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230507213433"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Garp_and_Sengoku.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Sengoku blaming Garp for Luffy's actions in <a href="/wiki/Impel_Down" title="Impel Down">Impel Down</a>.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>He later visited Ace in Impel Down. Upon Ace's request to die, Garp merely told him that his death would not stop Whitebeard. They later discussed family issues such as Ace and Luffy's turning to the life of piracy instead of becoming Marines. Ace also told Garp that he only considered Whitebeard as his true father.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">[87]</a></sup>
</p><p>Back at <a href="/wiki/Marineford" title="Marineford">Marineford</a>, Garp was informed that Luffy broke into Impel Down and was rather amused about it, even proud. <a href="/wiki/Sengoku" title="Sengoku">Sengoku</a> was furious and said that if Garp was not a hero to the Marines, he would have him punished for his family's actions. Garp just laughed and stated that an old man's life could not atone for his family's actions.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">[88]</a></sup><br style="clear:both;">
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Marineford_Arc">Marineford Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D59&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Three hours before <a href="/wiki/Portgas_D._Ace" title="Portgas D. Ace">Ace</a> was to be executed, Garp walked with <a href="/wiki/Sengoku" title="Sengoku">Sengoku</a> to the execution platform. Sengoku told him that he would tell the public everything and Garp did not express any objections. As Sengoku began his public announcement on the execution platform, <a href="/wiki/Tsuru" title="Tsuru">Tsuru</a> told Garp that it was not his fault. Garp just laughed and said that women get so sentimental at times like these. Once Sengoku revealed that Ace was truly the son of <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a>, Garp remembered the time when Roger personally begged him to protect his unborn child.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">[89]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/17/Garp_Grieving_Over_Ace%27s_Condition.png/revision/latest?cb=20230601052749" class="image"><img alt="Garp Grieving Over Ace's Condition" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Garp Grieving Over Ace's Condition.png" data-image-key="Garp_Grieving_Over_Ace%27s_Condition.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/17/Garp_Grieving_Over_Ace%27s_Condition.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230601052749"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/17/Garp_Grieving_Over_Ace%27s_Condition.png/revision/latest?cb=20230601052749" class="image"><img alt="Garp Grieving Over Ace's Condition" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/17/Garp_Grieving_Over_Ace%27s_Condition.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230601052749" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Garp Grieving Over Ace's Condition.png" data-image-key="Garp_Grieving_Over_Ace%27s_Condition.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/17/Garp_Grieving_Over_Ace%27s_Condition.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230601052749"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Garp_Grieving_Over_Ace%27s_Condition.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Garp grieving about how Ace ended up.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After the war began, Garp sat with Ace and Sengoku on top of the execution platform, upset at the present events. He stated that while he felt no sorrow for scoundrels, he felt differently when it came to Ace, who was family. Garp bitterly lamented that both Ace and <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a> did not become Marines.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">[90]</a></sup>
</p><p>Upon Luffy's arrival at Marineford, Garp was utterly shocked. Nevertheless, he managed to calm down long enough to comment on the viability of the motley little band that Luffy had assembled at Impel Down as part of Ace's rescue effort. Later, when Sengoku revealed Luffy's status as the son of Dragon the Revolutionary, Garp stated that with the infamy and power Luffy had acquired, such knowledge being brought to the general public hardly made a difference.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a4/Garp_Punches_Marco.png/revision/latest?cb=20230617140406" class="image"><img alt="Garp Punches Marco" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Garp Punches Marco.png" data-image-key="Garp_Punches_Marco.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a4/Garp_Punches_Marco.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230617140406"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a4/Garp_Punches_Marco.png/revision/latest?cb=20230617140406" class="image"><img alt="Garp Punches Marco" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a4/Garp_Punches_Marco.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230617140406" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Garp Punches Marco.png" data-image-key="Garp_Punches_Marco.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a4/Garp_Punches_Marco.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230617140406"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Garp_Punches_Marco.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Garp punching Marco in his phoenix form.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After Luffy was hurled over the siege wall and stood before the three admirals, Garp was shown to be worried about his grandson. He was later seen with Sengoku, getting ready to participate in the battle. Garp later punched <a href="/wiki/Marco" title="Marco">Marco</a>, who had transformed into his <a href="/wiki/Tori_Tori_no_Mi,_Model:_Phoenix" title="Tori Tori no Mi, Model: Phoenix">Phoenix form</a>, while he was trying to save Ace. Garp then challenged the <a href="/wiki/Whitebeard_Pirates" title="Whitebeard Pirates">Whitebeard Pirates</a>, saying that they would have to kill him before they could reach Ace.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">[91]</a></sup> When Luffy released a massive burst of <a href="/wiki/Haki/Observation_Haki" title="Haki/Observation Haki">Supreme King Haki</a>, Garp said he knew his grandson had that kind of power inside him.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">[92]</a></sup>
</p><p>When Luffy came close to reaching Ace, thanks to <a href="/wiki/Inazuma" title="Inazuma">Inazuma</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Choki_Choki_no_Mi" title="Choki Choki no Mi">powers</a>, Garp himself confronted him. He smashed part of the bridge in the process, saying that he could not let Luffy pass. He again complained about Luffy and Ace becoming pirates instead of Marines and declared that he considered them enemies.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">[93]</a></sup>
</p><p>As he was about to hit Luffy, he recalled Ace's renewed desire to live and reminisced about when Ace and Luffy were both young. Finding himself unwilling to resist, Garp closed his eyes, missing his punch. Thus, he allowed Luffy to land a Gear 2 punch that sent him flying and smashing into the ground, much to the shock of the Marines watching him.<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">[94]</a></sup>
</p><p>Garp later dislodged himself, more or less unfazed, and rejoined the battle. After witnessing Ace being pierced from behind by Akainu's <a href="/wiki/Magu_Magu_no_Mi" title="Magu Magu no Mi">magma fist</a>, Garp flew into a rage, prompting Sengoku to stop him, grabbing his head from behind and slamming him to the ground. Coughing up blood, Garp snarled that Sengoku should keep him down tight or he would murder Sakazuki. Sengoku responded by calling Garp a fool. When Ace died, Garp wept over the loss of his grandson.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">[95]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/99/Garp_and_Sengoku_vs_Blackbeard.png/revision/latest?cb=20130307084551" class="image"><img alt="Garp and Sengoku vs Blackbeard" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Garp and Sengoku vs Blackbeard.png" data-image-key="Garp_and_Sengoku_vs_Blackbeard.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/99/Garp_and_Sengoku_vs_Blackbeard.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20130307084551"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/99/Garp_and_Sengoku_vs_Blackbeard.png/revision/latest?cb=20130307084551" class="image"><img alt="Garp and Sengoku vs Blackbeard" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/99/Garp_and_Sengoku_vs_Blackbeard.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20130307084551" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Garp and Sengoku vs Blackbeard.png" data-image-key="Garp_and_Sengoku_vs_Blackbeard.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/99/Garp_and_Sengoku_vs_Blackbeard.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20130307084551"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Garp_and_Sengoku_vs_Blackbeard.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Garp and Sengoku battling Blackbeard.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When Whitebeard began attacking Marineford Headquarters after the death of Ace, Garp commented that Newgate was putting an end to this era, which he welcomed. As Whitebeard lost his life at the hands of the <a href="/wiki/Blackbeard_Pirates" title="Blackbeard Pirates">Blackbeard Pirates</a>, Garp watched with a grim expression. After acquiring the <a href="/wiki/Gura_Gura_no_Mi" title="Gura Gura no Mi">Gura Gura no Mi</a> from Whitebeard's corpse, Blackbeard commented to both Garp and Sengoku that their age was over, much like Whitebeard's.
</p><p>Later, he heard someone yelling to everyone. He saw Koby standing in front of Admiral Akainu, calling for an end to the war. Upon seeing Shanks making an appearance at Marineford, Garp made a snarling comment about the pirate who influenced Luffy into the path of piracy. When Sengoku announced that the war was over, Garp stood down along with the rest of the Marines.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Post-War_Arc">Post-War Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D60&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/79/Garp%27s_Homecoming.png/revision/latest?cb=20120831104859" class="image"><img alt="Garp's Homecoming" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Garp's Homecoming.png" data-image-key="Garp%27s_Homecoming.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/79/Garp%27s_Homecoming.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20120831104859"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/79/Garp%27s_Homecoming.png/revision/latest?cb=20120831104859" class="image"><img alt="Garp's Homecoming" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/79/Garp%27s_Homecoming.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20120831104859" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Garp's Homecoming.png" data-image-key="Garp%27s_Homecoming.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/79/Garp%27s_Homecoming.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20120831104859"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Garp%27s_Homecoming.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Garp, Makino, and Dadan reflecting over the war.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>With the end of the war, Garp took up a station in <a href="/wiki/Foosha_Village" title="Foosha Village">Foosha Village</a> on <a href="/wiki/Dawn_Island" title="Dawn Island">Dawn Island</a>, seeing it as necessary to protect the island with the increase in pirate activities. After returning to the village, he took a beating from <a href="/wiki/Curly_Dadan" title="Curly Dadan">Curly Dadan</a> for letting Ace die until <a href="/wiki/Makino" title="Makino">Makino</a> intervened. Makino tried to tell Dadan that Garp was suffering the most from Ace's death, but Dadan replied that the one suffering the most was Luffy. After Dadan calmed down, Garp informed <a href="/wiki/Woop_Slap" title="Woop Slap">Woop Slap</a> that Luffy escaped Marineford in a <a href="/wiki/Polar_Tang" title="Polar Tang">submarine</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">[96]</a></sup>
</p><p>It was later revealed that both him and Sengoku stepped down from the Marines. However, both would remain for the sake of rearing up new young Marines.<sup id="cite_ref-Discussion_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Discussion-3">[3]</a></sup><br style="clear:both;">
</p><p><small>
</small></p><small><hr></small><small></small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>The following events are <a href="/wiki/Canon#Non-Canon" title="Canon">Non-Canon</a> and therefore not considered part of the <a href="/wiki/Canon" title="Canon">Canon</a> story.</b></i></span>
</p><small><hr></small>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Dressrosa_Saga">Dressrosa Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D61&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="One_Piece_Film:_Z">One Piece Film: Z</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D62&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6a/Garp_Firs_Island.png/revision/latest?cb=20140722072332" class="image"><img alt="Garp Firs Island" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Garp Firs Island.png" data-image-key="Garp_Firs_Island.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6a/Garp_Firs_Island.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20140722072332"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6a/Garp_Firs_Island.png/revision/latest?cb=20140722072332" class="image"><img alt="Garp Firs Island" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6a/Garp_Firs_Island.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20140722072332" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Garp Firs Island.png" data-image-key="Garp_Firs_Island.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6a/Garp_Firs_Island.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20140722072332"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Garp_Firs_Island.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Garp at Firs Island.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After <a href="/wiki/Firs_Island" title="Firs Island">Firs Island</a> was destroyed by <a href="/wiki/Z" title="Z">Z</a>, Garp appeared on a Marine battleship along with Koby and Helmeppo, and revealed to them the existence of Z. Later, after the destruction of <a href="/wiki/Secon_Island" title="Secon Island">Secon Island</a>, he and Sengoku explained to them Z's past.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">[97]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Whole_Cake_Island_Saga">Whole Cake Island Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D63&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Marine_Rookie_Arc">Marine Rookie Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D64&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Garp was in his office when he received a call from Vice Admiral <a href="/wiki/Prodi" title="Prodi">Prodi</a>, who was angry about the new transfer <a href="/wiki/Grount" class="mw-redirect" title="Grount">Grount</a>'s actions in his base on <a href="/wiki/Fron_Island" title="Fron Island">Fron Island</a>. Garp simply asked Prodi to take care of Grount.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">[98]</a></sup>
<small>
</small></p><small><hr></small><small></small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>Concludes non-canon section.</b></i></span>
</p><small><hr></small>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Levely_Arc">Levely Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D65&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/74/Neptune_Family_Arrives_At_The_Red_Port.png/revision/latest?cb=20230408051539" class="image"><img alt="Neptune Family Arrives At The Red Port" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="112" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Neptune Family Arrives At The Red Port.png" data-image-key="Neptune_Family_Arrives_At_The_Red_Port.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/74/Neptune_Family_Arrives_At_The_Red_Port.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230408051539"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/74/Neptune_Family_Arrives_At_The_Red_Port.png/revision/latest?cb=20230408051539" class="image"><img alt="Neptune Family Arrives At The Red Port" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/74/Neptune_Family_Arrives_At_The_Red_Port.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230408051539" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="112" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Neptune Family Arrives At The Red Port.png" data-image-key="Neptune_Family_Arrives_At_The_Red_Port.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/74/Neptune_Family_Arrives_At_The_Red_Port.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230408051539"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Neptune_Family_Arrives_At_The_Red_Port.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Garp escorts the Neptune Family to Mary Geoise.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After the <a href="/wiki/Neptune_Family" title="Neptune Family">Neptune Family</a> arrived at the surface to the Red Port at the Red Line, Garp escorted them to the bondola. He commented on <a href="/wiki/Shirahoshi" title="Shirahoshi">Shirahoshi</a>'s beauty that exceeds everyone's expectations when the media was taking pictures of her. When he met <a href="/wiki/Sterry" title="Sterry">Sterry</a>, Garp claimed that he did not know him and openly insulted him before half-heartedly taking it back after he was told that Sterry was the king of <a href="/wiki/Goa_Kingdom" title="Goa Kingdom">Goa Kingdom</a>. As the <a href="/wiki/Neptune" title="Neptune">Neptune</a> Family rode on the bondola, Garp waved one last time to Shirahoshi.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">[99]</a></sup>
</p><p>After the Marines intercepted a communication between <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a>, Garp remained calm despite the fact that the two <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Emperors</a> had a grudge against Luffy. He then spoke with <a href="/wiki/Hina" title="Hina">Hina</a> about a <a href="/wiki/Rocks_Pirates" title="Rocks Pirates">pirate group</a> prominent before Roger's era during which suggested that he got the distinction of "Hero of the Marines" from dealing with them while Garp noted that he could not imagine what the Marines would do if said crew were to come back into power.<sup id="cite_ref-c907_31-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c907-31">[31]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Wano_Country_Saga">Wano Country Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D66&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

</small></p><small><hr></small><small></small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>The following events are <a href="/wiki/Canon#Non-Canon" title="Canon">Non-Canon</a> and therefore not considered part of the <a href="/wiki/Canon" title="Canon">Canon</a> story.</b></i></span>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="One_Piece:_Stampede">One Piece: Stampede</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D67&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/29/Garp_And_Sengoku_Talks_About_Douglas_Bullet.png/revision/latest?cb=20210726121057" class="image"><img alt="Garp And Sengoku Talks About Douglas Bullet" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Garp And Sengoku Talks About Douglas Bullet.png" data-image-key="Garp_And_Sengoku_Talks_About_Douglas_Bullet.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/29/Garp_And_Sengoku_Talks_About_Douglas_Bullet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20210726121057"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/29/Garp_And_Sengoku_Talks_About_Douglas_Bullet.png/revision/latest?cb=20210726121057" class="image"><img alt="Garp And Sengoku Talks About Douglas Bullet" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/29/Garp_And_Sengoku_Talks_About_Douglas_Bullet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20210726121057" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Garp And Sengoku Talks About Douglas Bullet.png" data-image-key="Garp_And_Sengoku_Talks_About_Douglas_Bullet.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/29/Garp_And_Sengoku_Talks_About_Douglas_Bullet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20210726121057"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Garp_And_Sengoku_Talks_About_Douglas_Bullet.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Garp and Sengoku talks about Douglas Bullet.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Garp appears at the Marine Headquarters listening to <a href="/wiki/Brannew" title="Brannew">Brannew</a>'s talk about <a href="/wiki/Douglas_Bullet" title="Douglas Bullet">Douglas Bullet</a> and the current situation on <a href="/wiki/Delta_Island" title="Delta Island">Delta Island</a>. Then, he meets Sengoku outside, with whom he talks about Bullet's past.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">[100]</a></sup>
<small>
</small></p><small><hr></small><small></small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>Concludes non-canon section.</b></i></span>
</p><small><hr></small>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Wano_Country_Arc">Wano Country Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D68&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After the Levely, Garp went to <a href="/wiki/Fish-Man_Island" title="Fish-Man Island">Fish-Man Island</a> with Neptune and his family. While conversing with Neptune, Garp mentioned an incident involving <a href="/wiki/Arabasta_Kingdom" title="Arabasta Kingdom">Arabasta</a> that occurred after they left Mary Geoise.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">[101]</a></sup> While leaving Fish-Man Island, Garp read a report, being informed of the <a href="/wiki/Pirate_Alliance" title="Pirate Alliance">alliance</a> between Kaidou and Big Mom, much to his annoyance.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">[102]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Final_Saga">Final Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D69&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Egghead_Arc">Egghead Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D70&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Weeks later, Koby was reported to have been abducted by the <a href="/wiki/Blackbeard_Pirates" title="Blackbeard Pirates">Blackbeard Pirates</a>, so Garp sailed to <a href="/wiki/G-14" title="G-14">G-14</a> before heading to <a href="/wiki/Hachinosu" title="Hachinosu">Hachinosu</a>. Vice Admiral <a href="/wiki/Doll" title="Doll">Doll</a> tried to dissuade Garp from taking Helmeppo and starting a fight with an Emperor, but Garp ignored her protests and yelled for Helmeppo to join him in rescuing Koby.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">[103]</a></sup> Having recruited members of <a href="/wiki/SWORD" title="SWORD">SWORD</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tashigi" title="Tashigi">Tashigi</a> for his mission, the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a> departed to Hachinosu. Upon SWORD beginning their attack on the island and Garp's ship approaching it, the ship was launched from the sea to above the island. Telling the pirates how important Koby is to the future of the Marines and himself, he infused his fist in <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a> and attacked the island with <i>Galaxy Impact</i> and decimated the surrounding area.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">[104]</a></sup> 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/70/Blue_Hole.png/revision/latest?cb=20240811020812" class="image"><img alt="Blue Hole" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="185" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Blue Hole.png" data-image-key="Blue_Hole.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/70/Blue_Hole.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240811020812"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/70/Blue_Hole.png/revision/latest?cb=20240811020812" class="image"><img alt="Blue Hole" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/70/Blue_Hole.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240811020812" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="185" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Blue Hole.png" data-image-key="Blue_Hole.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/70/Blue_Hole.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240811020812"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Blue_Hole.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Garp slams Kuzan into the ground.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Garp then landed safely and stated he was disappointed that he had lost his touch with his attack, much to the shock and surprise of the Blackbeard Pirates. Garp was then confronted by <a href="/wiki/Kuzan" title="Kuzan">Kuzan</a>, who froze <a href="/wiki/Hibari" title="Hibari">Hibari</a> and stated he would not let Koby escape. Garp then demanded that Kuzan unfreeze Hibari, set Koby free, and return to the Marines, but Kuzan rejected his demands, stating he always loved that Garp did what he wanted. Kuzan then froze Garp with <i>Ice Ball</i>, asking Garp if he could kill his old protégé to protect his new one, but Garp only replied he had told Kuzan that he should live in the moment and that wavering would be a sign of weakness. He then imbued his hand with Armament and Supreme King Haki and grabbed Kuzan mid-air, slamming him into the ground below with <i>Blue Hole</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">[105]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6e/Garp_wounded_and_surrounded_by_Blackbeard_Pirates.png/revision/latest?cb=20241013020339" class="image"><img alt="Garp wounded and surrounded by Blackbeard Pirates" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Garp wounded and surrounded by Blackbeard Pirates.png" data-image-key="Garp_wounded_and_surrounded_by_Blackbeard_Pirates.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6e/Garp_wounded_and_surrounded_by_Blackbeard_Pirates.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20241013020339"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6e/Garp_wounded_and_surrounded_by_Blackbeard_Pirates.png/revision/latest?cb=20241013020339" class="image"><img alt="Garp wounded and surrounded by Blackbeard Pirates" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6e/Garp_wounded_and_surrounded_by_Blackbeard_Pirates.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20241013020339" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Garp wounded and surrounded by Blackbeard Pirates.png" data-image-key="Garp_wounded_and_surrounded_by_Blackbeard_Pirates.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6e/Garp_wounded_and_surrounded_by_Blackbeard_Pirates.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20241013020339"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Garp_wounded_and_surrounded_by_Blackbeard_Pirates.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Garp defeated and surrounded by the Blackbeard Pirates.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Garp threw <a href="/wiki/Sanjuan_Wolf" title="Sanjuan Wolf">Sanjuan Wolf</a> into the sea, which caused the Blackbeard Pirates to rush in to save him from drowning. <a href="/wiki/Vasco_Shot" title="Vasco Shot">Vasco Shot</a> then tried <a href="/wiki/Gabu_Gabu_no_Mi" title="Gabu Gabu no Mi">burning</a> Garp, but the old man merely used random pirates as human shields. <a href="/wiki/Shiryu" title="Shiryu">Shiryu</a> attempted to stab Koby while he was <a href="/wiki/Suke_Suke_no_Mi" title="Suke Suke no Mi">invisible</a>, but Garp stepped in front of him and took the attack instead. Kuzan then returned and resumed battling.<sup id="cite_ref-c1087_43-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1087-43">[43]</a></sup> As <a href="/wiki/Avalo_Pizarro" title="Avalo Pizarro">Avalo Pizarro</a> was about to crush Garp's ship and all the marines and escaped slaves on it with his <a href="/wiki/Shima_Shima_no_Mi" title="Shima Shima no Mi">massive hand of rock and soil</a>, Garp ordered Koby, Helmeppo, and Grus to deal with the hand while he attacked the giant stone skull, delivering serious damage to Pizarro. As Koby and the rest of SWORD successfully escaped the island, Garp was pierced though the chest again, this time by Kuzan's ice. Garp smiled as he told everyone via the <a href="/wiki/Den_Den_Mushi" title="Den Den Mushi">Den Den Mushi</a> to never forget they were the future of the Marines as Wolf, Shiryu, Pizarro, Shot and Kuzan closed in on him. Garp then started laughing and the transmission ended.<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">[106]</a></sup> 
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Elbaph_Arc">Elbaph Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D71&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/11/Garp_Imprisoned_on_Hachinosu.png/revision/latest?cb=20240915150731" class="image"><img alt="Garp Imprisoned on Hachinosu" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="154" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Garp Imprisoned on Hachinosu.png" data-image-key="Garp_Imprisoned_on_Hachinosu.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/11/Garp_Imprisoned_on_Hachinosu.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240915150731"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/11/Garp_Imprisoned_on_Hachinosu.png/revision/latest?cb=20240915150731" class="image"><img alt="Garp Imprisoned on Hachinosu" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/11/Garp_Imprisoned_on_Hachinosu.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240915150731" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="154" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Garp Imprisoned on Hachinosu.png" data-image-key="Garp_Imprisoned_on_Hachinosu.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/11/Garp_Imprisoned_on_Hachinosu.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240915150731"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Garp_Imprisoned_on_Hachinosu.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Garp Imprisoned on Hachinosu</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Garp survived Kuzan's attack and was subsequently taken prisoner by the Blackbeard Pirates. Teach was excited to have a superior bargaining chip than Koby.<sup id="cite_ref-c1126_17-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1126-17">[17]</a></sup><br style="clear:both;">
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Adaptation_Differences">Adaptation Differences</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D72&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Anime_Differences">Anime Differences</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D73&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In the anime, the Marines accompanying Garp identified him, not Nami immediately and she only calls him that after hearing his name.
</p><p>In the anime, Garp attacks <a href="/wiki/Jesus_Burgess" title="Jesus Burgess">Jesus Burgess</a> when he moves to strike Sengoku while he is distracted. After the war ended, he orders the soldiers to gather the wounded so no one else would die.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b9/Garp_Punishes_Luffy_and_Ace.png/revision/latest?cb=20230214040415" class="image"><img alt="Garp Punishes Luffy and Ace" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Garp Punishes Luffy and Ace.png" data-image-key="Garp_Punishes_Luffy_and_Ace.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b9/Garp_Punishes_Luffy_and_Ace.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230214040415"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b9/Garp_Punishes_Luffy_and_Ace.png/revision/latest?cb=20230214040415" class="image"><img alt="Garp Punishes Luffy and Ace" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b9/Garp_Punishes_Luffy_and_Ace.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230214040415" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Garp Punishes Luffy and Ace.png" data-image-key="Garp_Punishes_Luffy_and_Ace.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b9/Garp_Punishes_Luffy_and_Ace.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230214040415"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Garp_Punishes_Luffy_and_Ace.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Garp about to punish (or in this case, train) Luffy and Ace.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the anime, a young Luffy blurted out that the trio shared a promise over a shared drink. Garp overheard them boasting of their dreams to become pirates, leaving him infuriated. Garp then chases them out into the night, breaking down trees and rocks and beating them all to a pulp. Sabo exclaimed he was a monster. Afterwards, he casually leaves them, saying that he will not be so merciful next time. This was not shown in the manga. In the manga version, Garp was shown saying hello first before "training" them.<br style="clear:both;">
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Live-Action_Differences">Live-Action Differences</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D74&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In the live-action series, Garp's role in the story is changed drastically from the manga. Garp's relationship to Luffy is made clear much earlier than the manga, with Zoro, Nami, and Usopp learning that he is Luffy's grandfather as early as their first sail on the <a href="/wiki/Going_Merry" title="Going Merry">Going Merry</a>. Garp chases the Straw Hat Pirates across the East Blue, from Shells Town to Cocomi Islands, instead of meeting them after the events at Enies Lobby. Garp is also much more dedicated to capturing Luffy and ending his pirate career before it begins.
</p><p>When Garp's ship intercepts the Going Merry, Luffy manages to deter the Marines by bouncing one of their cannon balls back at their mast as the Straw Hats escape through a fog.
</p><p>After the Straw Hats arrive at the Baratie, Garp enlists the help of Dracula Mihawk to bring Luffy in alive. When Mihawk refuses to, even with the threat of revoking his status as Warlord, Garp is irate. He later talks to Koby about the Warlords and expresses his disdain for the World Government's decisions and why he remains a Vice-Admiral.
</p><p>Garp arrives at the <a href="/wiki/Baratie" title="Baratie">Baratie</a> to ask <a href="/wiki/Zeff" title="Zeff">Zeff</a> about Luffy's whereabouts. Garp confesses to Zeff why he is insistent on capturing Luffy.
</p><p>As Straw Hats celebrate their victory over <a href="/wiki/Arlong" title="Arlong">Arlong</a> and his <a href="/wiki/Arlong_Pirates" title="Arlong Pirates">crew</a>, Garp and the Marines arrive at Coco Village. Garp plans to bring the Straw Hats in, but Luffy refuses to yield. Garp and Luffy fight, with the former dominating the battle. After seeing Roger's own determination and spirit in him, Garp changes his mind on arresting Luffy and instead orders his Marines to hunt the stragglers of Arlong's crew. He later receives his grandson's first bounty, impressed by how far he has come.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Filler_Battles">Filler Battles</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D76&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>Monkey D. Garp vs. <a href="/wiki/Jesus_Burgess" title="Jesus Burgess">Jesus Burgess</a></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_Concepts">Early Concepts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D77&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 172px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 172px; height: 172px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a7/Luffy%27s_Grandfather_in_Romance_Dawn.png/revision/latest?cb=20240115020607" class="image"><img alt="Luffy's Grandfather in Romance Dawn" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="150" height="125" data-image-name="Luffy's Grandfather in Romance Dawn.png" data-image-key="Luffy%27s_Grandfather_in_Romance_Dawn.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a7/Luffy%27s_Grandfather_in_Romance_Dawn.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20240115020607" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Luffy's grandfather from <i>Romance Dawn V.2.</i>
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 172px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 172px; height: 172px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/ad/Luffy%27s_Grandfather_Romance_Dawn_Anime.png/revision/latest?cb=20191021014020" class="image"><img alt="Luffy's Grandfather Romance Dawn Anime" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="117" height="150" data-image-name="Luffy's Grandfather Romance Dawn Anime.png" data-image-key="Luffy%27s_Grandfather_Romance_Dawn_Anime.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/ad/Luffy%27s_Grandfather_Romance_Dawn_Anime.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/117?cb=20191021014020" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Luffy's grandfather in the <i>Romance Dawn</i> anime special.
</div></span></div>
<p>While unnamed, Garp was introduced in <i><a href="/wiki/Romance_Dawn,_Version_2" title="Romance Dawn, Version 2">Romance Dawn, Version 2</a></i> (featured in <b><a href="/wiki/Shonen_Jump" title="Shonen Jump">Weekly Shonen Jump</a> magazine</b> itself) as <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a>'s grandfather. For a long time, it was first thought that Luffy's unnamed Grandfather was a sole addition to Romance Dawn V.2.
</p><p>Some aspects of his character remain from <i>Romance Dawn V.2</i>. He is as hot tempered as ever and intolerant of Luffy's antics. Like the final version, he was determined to make Luffy follow in his footsteps, however here he is a pirate captain, the complete opposite of his current occupation. Both stories have in return Luffy completely rejecting the idea of following in his grandfather's footsteps. Garp now occasionally wears a dog hat and compared to his chubby <i>Romance Dawn V.2</i> version, his upper body is much more muscular.
</p><p>One feature carried over from Luffy's grandfather from <i>V.2</i> to the final version of Garp was the scar on his left eye. Also, Luffy got both his hat and the Devil fruit he ate from his grandfather in <i>V.2</i>, not Shanks. According to Oda the reason for not featuring Shanks was that he wanted Shanks to be kept a secret until <i>One Piece</i> was serialized so he would have a greater impact.<sup id="cite_ref-RD1_107-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RD1-107">[107]</a></sup>
</p><p>When <i>V.2</i> was adapted into <a href="/wiki/Episode_907" title="Episode 907">Episode 907</a> of the anime as a celebration of the series' 20th anniversary, he had Garp's muscular physique instead of the chubby appearance he had in the manga. He also had Garp's voice actors.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D83&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Garp is the first <a href="/wiki/Vice_Admiral" title="Vice Admiral">Vice Admiral</a> to be introduced in the series, first appearing in a cover story</li>
<li>He and <a href="/wiki/Sengoku" title="Sengoku">Sengoku</a> are also the only known Marines to possess <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a>.
<ul><li>He is also the first Marine to showcase it and its advanced form.</li></ul></li>
<li>Garp's wife has not been named, but the supplement <i><a href="/wiki/Grand_Line_Times" class="mw-redirect" title="Grand Line Times">Grand Line Times</a></i> left a "?" in place of her in their family tree.</li>
<li>Initially, Garp smoked cigars,<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">[108]</a></sup> but in later appearances, he stopped doing it.</li>
<li>In the anime, Garp said he has eaten a total of 842 donuts without sleeping or taking a break because he was trying to beat a world record.<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">[109]</a></sup></li>
<li>Aside from <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a> himself, Garp is the only <a href="/wiki/Romance_Dawn,_Version_2" title="Romance Dawn, Version 2">Romance Dawn V.2</a> character to actually appear in the storyline.</li>
<li>Garp's <a href="/wiki/Laughter_Style" title="Laughter Style">laughter style</a> is that he adds either "Bwa" or "Wa" before the haha part. This is somewhat unique as most characters only stick with one laughter style (the only other character sharing this distinction being <a href="/wiki/Dracule_Mihawk" title="Dracule Mihawk">Dracule Mihawk</a>).</li>
<li>Garp appears to have a dog animal-theme, as shown by his mask and <a href="/wiki/Garp%27s_ship" class="mw-redirect" title="Garp's ship">his ship</a>.</li>
<li>In the 4th, 5th and 7th <a href="/wiki/Popularity_Polls" title="Popularity Polls">fan polls</a> of most popular characters, Garp was ranked the 50th, 74th and 44th, respectively.</li>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Magazine_Vol.5" title="One Piece Magazine Vol.5"><i>One Piece Magazine</i> Vol.5</a>, Oda drew a "what-if" illustration of <a href="/wiki/Portgas_D._Ace" title="Portgas D. Ace">Ace</a>, Luffy, and <a href="/wiki/Sabo" title="Sabo">Sabo</a> as Marines. Garp was seen wielding a pair of katana swords.<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">[110]</a></sup></li>
<li>Garp's favorite foods are <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/senbei" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:senbei">senbei</a> and curry,<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_6-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-6">[6]</a></sup> and his least favorite food is bell pepper.<sup id="cite_ref-vc2_25-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vc2-25">[25]</a></sup></li>
<li>During their youths, Garp's looks were strikingly similar to Luffy's own, and, in an ironic twist of fate, Garp and Luffy would have a similar appearance to the former's long-term rival Gol D. Roger, before the latter appeared more so like his son Ace as he got older.</li>
<li>Garp's hobby is senbei party.<sup id="cite_ref-vc2_25-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vc2-25">[25]</a></sup></li>
<li>Garp's animal resemblance is a St. Bernard.<sup id="cite_ref-vc2_25-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vc2-25">[25]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="SBS-Based_Trivia">SBS-Based Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMonkey_D._Garp%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D84&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>A fan pointed out the fact that despite Garp's few appearances, his trademark scar has disappeared 25 times if counted up to <a href="/wiki/Volume_58" title="Volume 58">Volume 58</a>. In response to the statement above, <a href="/wiki/Eiichiro_Oda" title="Eiichiro Oda">Oda</a> joked that "if an enemy he hates is around, his scar tingles, and it will float up" and that Garp's "true form" may be the scar-less one, but he also points out that this is not proved anywhere.<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">[111]</a></sup></li>
<li>According to Oda, the reason Garp's "Fist of Love" can injure his <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi">rubber-bodied</a> grandson Luffy is not due to <a href="/wiki/Haki/Armament_Haki" title="Haki/Armament Haki">Armament Haki</a> but simply "love".<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">[112]</a></sup></li></ul>
